# DONE

Archive of completed YOLOmux work, newest first. Concise by design — the full implementation detail (file/symbol, fix, tests) lives in the git commit history on `main`.

Unless an entry says otherwise, every item shipped with the standard check gate green (`tools/check.py`: py_compile, `static_build.py --check`, both `node --check`, `node tests/layout_url.test.js`, full pytest, `git diff --check`). Entries call out only verification that goes BEYOND that gate (live user confirmation, focused browser repros, notable test counts).

- Completed and removed `DOIT.audit-coverage-integrity-refactor.md` (self-audit of this session's coverage-integrity code). The coverage-overlap definition (a self-join) and the disjoint-seam clip rule were each implemented in two places; both now have ONE owner — `StatsStore._coverage_overlap_pairs` (used by the durable-repair gate and the integrity self-check) and `StatsStore._clip_disjoint_intervals` (used by both the serve-time bound and the durable repair, which now loads→clips→writes-back through the shared rule). The sliding-axis render cadence is documented as a display constant (round, not an odd poll). `tests/test_statsd.py` (31 coverage/handoff/repair/integrity/property tests) green; test self-joins kept as intentional independent verification; `static_build.py --check` clean.

- YO!stats coverage-integrity flakiness fixed (backend landed; `DOIT.yostats-coverage-integrity-and-validation-regime.md` retained for the validation-regime hardening). YO!stats charts blanked flakily at 16h/24h because statsd restart/owner-handoff boundary overlaps persisted in `stats_coverage_intervals` (proven on the live DB: 35 overlapping pairs = 7 per family across a 8-owner PID chain, each new owner backfilling a first sample seconds before the outgoing owner's finalized end) and the client rejected the whole malformed multi-family payload. `_bounded_intervals` coalesced only within an epoch; it now clips cross-epoch overlaps at serve time (later owner authoritative), the write path ends the prior owner's interval when a new owner opens, an idempotent on-open durable repair heals pre-existing overlaps, and a read-only `coverage_integrity_report()` self-check reports violations. The client now degrades per-family (count bound caps, malformed family dropped with a Logs warning) instead of blanking every chart, and the false "Backfill pending" (a symptom of the rejection, since the durable marker was already complete) is resolved. Regression tests: unit seam-clip, write-handoff, durable repair, a 12-seed property test under random owner churn, backfill-status, integrity-report, and client per-family degrade; verified read-only against the live DB (16h/24h/1h/30m serve 0 overlaps/0 inversions). Full `tools/check.py` gate green (all five lanes). Durable repair applies on the next statsd restart; serve-time clipping renders correctly meanwhile.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.tab-switch-highlight-first.md`. Tab switches now flip the new tab's active chrome and focus ring synchronously in the input frame while the heavy xterm/content work defers behind a rAF, through the one shared `activatePaneTab` funnel used by pane-tab clicks, keyboard cycling, and the Tabs menu. Rapid cycling coalesces content to the final target (generation-guarded) so intermediate tabs waste no xterm work, and the previous tab's content never lingers under the new highlight. A paint-order lock in the browser gate (slowed-phase-2 hook) asserts highlight-before-content and fails if anyone reorders it. Merged from an isolated worktree; static/node/browser lanes green.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.resolution-choices-simplify.md`. The Resolution picker is simplified to AUTO + 1s/10s/60s/300s (filtered per range), decoupled from the AUTO bucket set; a stale out-of-set persisted override rounds up to the nearest coarser valid choice, and an over-budget explicit override is capped to the finest within-budget choice (a 600-point cap) while the dropdown still shows the requested value. The never-regress resolution Selenium sweep was rewritten to the new per-range sets on both YO!stats and YO!cost; Node tests cover the new universe, clamp, and point-cap. Verified with a real browser.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.resolution-change-loading-feedback.md`. Changing Resolution now reflects the target label optimistically within a frame and shows the existing shared dimmed/centered loading overlay when a fetch is needed (no second mechanism), reverts the control with a danger toast on failure (generation-guarded, localized across 19 locales), and swaps instantly with no overlay when the resolution is already cached. A new `statsResolution` notification policy row and Node regressions cover the overlay/revert and cached-instant paths.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.yocost-narrow-xscroll-last-resort.md`. At extreme-narrow widths the YO!cost By-Agent cards now scroll horizontally (contained `overflow-x:auto` + min-inline-size) instead of squishing/overlapping, while normal-narrow still reflows to two-column cards and wide keeps the full table; scoped so the char-wrap-locked model/calculation tables stay contained. A Selenium test asserts 260px scrolls with no char-wrap or pane scrollbar and 360px reflows; the char-wrap detector still sweeps 260/360/720/1200.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.cpu-missing-chunk-and-red-nodata-boxes.md`. Research found no CPU recording hole — coverage was continuous from the first-ever sample, broken only by 1–2s owner-churn epoch micro-breaks mis-rendered as 1px red hairlines plus a genuine never-recorded prefix. Sub-bucket micro-gaps are now dropped (`debugGraphMeaningfulCoverageGaps`) while genuine and never-recorded-prefix uncovered spans render as one full-span red no-data box (`.js-debug-history-no-data-range`, both themes), cross-family global coverage fallback is removed so a family's pre-first-sample window shows its own red box, and gap hover reads "No data recorded" (19 locales). Node regression verified failing without the change; browser geometry green.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.logs-hide-info-by-default.md`. The YO!stats Logs tab now defaults to warning+error visible with info+debug hidden but one click away and persisted (`logLevels`); the recording buffer is unchanged so enabling a level reveals its buffered entries. Node and browser regressions assert the default, `aria-pressed=false` for hidden levels, togglability, and a persisted selection honored across reload.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.pricing-catalog-seed-fetch-and-unpriced-dropdown.md`. Unpriced usage now shows three always-visible accounting rows and a default-closed accessible provider/model/class/token disclosure instead of one run-on list. Packaged seed revision 2 prices current GPT-5.6 and Claude families offline from their actual provider availability dates; structured provider tables and schema-validated machine JSON refresh daily from the elected owner with jitter/backoff, conservative aliases are visibly inferred, and immutable prior evidence guarantees a partial refresh cannot reduce coverage. Exact tests cover fresh historical pricing, parser failure transactions, layering/priority, inference labels, carry-forward warnings/nondecreasing coverage, scheduling, and 260–1200px dark/light disclosure geometry. On restarted 8881, catalog revision 6 is fresh with seed revision 2 and a scheduled refresh; July 11 GPT-5.6 Sol/Terra and Claude Fable/Opus usage resolves at expected rates.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.uploads-to-tmp-per-yolomux-user.md`. Every terminal paste/drop and editor upload now uses one authenticated-identity owner under `/tmp/yolomux.<user>/uploads/<session>/`, with normalized components, 0700 private directories, exclusive 0600 files, collision suffixes, and refusal of symlink/non-directory/foreign-owner squatters. Existing references remain readable; configurable lazy retention defaults to seven days; editor Markdown receives the absolute transient path. Multi-user, concurrent-server, handler-identity, retention, permission, and generated-client regressions pass. An authenticated request through restarted 8881 created and read a correctly protected `/tmp/yolomux.keivenc/uploads/workqueue-live-qa/...` artifact, then removed it.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.yocost-seven-fixes-and-regression-locks.md`. Cost/System content consumes one responsive no-character-wrap shell with structured middle-truncated source paths and a generic multi-theme/width detector. Token hover reports actual bucket spans/sample counts; attributed atoms provide per-agent Input/Cache/All-billable while Output remains exact; dimension changes repaint both surfaces within one frame without refetching; loading uses the inactive-pane overlay; every range transition rebuilds/clamps shared resolution choices; and one fixed live-edge block consumes the exact shared agent-status pulse clock instead of moving markers. Permanent Selenium locks cover sparse history, reconciliation, sub-100ms switching, overlays, every range/tab, 260–1200px layouts, and pulse geometry/cadence. The final non-browser lane passed 2,240 tests in 195.62s and browser lane passed 471 with 5 skipped in 418.90s; restarted 8881 serves byte-identical bundles.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.yolomux-cpu-bursts-drag-jank-coverage-errors.md`. The API-process burst was the recursive indexed-repository discovery under session metadata, not indexd; it now runs only as a maintenance-priority protocol-2 jobd task while requests consume one asynchronous last-good snapshot. Explicit mid-backfill coverage is a retryable retained-chart state with bounded automatic recovery, malformed coverage remains an explicit Retry error, and every direct/scheduled YO!stats/YO!cost repaint defers and coalesces during pane drag. Expected client disconnects are counted without tracebacks and only a safe zero-byte legacy service DB is removed. The deterministic browser regressions cover pending-to-ready recovery, the 50 ms drag budget/no DOM replacement/single flush, and proportional left/right nested pane splits. Live 8881 verification measured the web process at 0.3% CPU with zero walker/scandir/lstat sample frames; jobd completed the new registered task, the legacy DB was absent, and the post-restart log had no new traceback, timeout, unknown-task, or disconnect exception.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.optimistic-ui-zippy-tabs-windows.md`. Pane-tab, Tabs-menu, cold-terminal placement, and tmux-window navigation now acknowledge locally within one animation frame before readiness/network work; shared dimmed connecting/reconnecting/switching/unavailable states provide Retry or visible rollback, and one topbar health indicator replaces silent repeated failures. Removing the old pre-visual ensure exposed a Dockview race in which a queued center fallback collapsed a newer edge split; the fallback now yields to the app-owned transaction and pane-edge intent comes from the shared percentage-based rectangle zones. The real-browser suite holds requests forever and fails them to pin the 50 ms acknowledgement, Retry/revert, health recovery, and exact 14%-inside left/right split geometries. The final eight-lane gate passed in 410.02 seconds and 8881 restarted as one listener with its expected unauthenticated 401.

- YO!stats navigation/history regressions now have end-to-end coverage for the three reported cases: 16h/24h views retain one continuous loading phase instead of repeatedly flashing `Loading older data`; three unknown usage classes reconcile provider-aware 24-hour cost uncertainty without the old all-or-nothing upper bound; and 30m keeps its resolution control even when a coarse coverage interval touches the left boundary. Related regressions pin one boot fetch, no passive request queue, hidden-to-visible catch-up only, continuously ready live-tail updates, 5m/15m SSE versus 30m+/fixed-history minute polling, and immediate short-range backfill. Servers Load/System ordering, persistence, narrow tables, and optimistic terminal navigation are included in the same browser gate.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.yostats-system-condensed-and-servers-load-chart.md`. System sampler families now share the fixed-layout table shell with Local services, keeping one-line family names and horizontal narrow-pane overflow; all 19 locale catalogs provide condensed visual headings with full tooltip/accessibility text, and unavailable history-query detail is one em dash. The independent 10-second `service_load` sampler reuses existing local-service resource status, stores CPU/RSS total/min/max/sample aggregates in the normal host-metrics buckets, preserves honest epoch gaps, and rolls up through statsd. The default-off Servers Load chart sits immediately after CPU, persists visibility, and renders palette/pattern-distinct service lines with CPU min/average/max hover. Verification: static build/check and `git diff --check`; all 15 Node shards; all 91 `test_statsd.py` tests; the independent-cadence app test; and focused narrow-System plus chart order/toggle/legend/hover/reload browser tests. The isolated implementation worktree did not restart or modify the live 8881 checkout.

- Completed and removed the async YO!stats coverage, graph-render, and CPU-audit queues. Protocol 20/schema 3 now records bounded per-family coverage intervals and sampler epochs atomically, models sleep/restart holes as honest gaps, bounds status carry-forward by epoch, and keeps legacy schema-2 databases read-only compatible. CPU, Agent Status, GPU, memory, and tokens have independent nonblocking owners at 1s, 10s, 10s, 60s, and 10s-active/60s-idle cadences; lower-frequency gauges are presentation-held at fine resolution without inventing stored samples or inflating totals. Graph controls are mounted/preserved across passive ticks, explicit toggles/range retries/sorts repaint immediately, ≤1h views animate only the bounded live cell, and coarser/hidden/history views stay static. Token palettes/patterns, zoom, cost age, and SSE demand are shared across YO!stats/YO!cost. The corrected CPU attribution found repeated Git metadata subprocess work—not directory enumeration—as the dominant old web-process cost; process-wide metadata single-flight/signatures and Finder in-flight coalescing reduced unchanged Git fanout from 8+ subprocesses to at most 2. A sustained >30%/5m CPU warning and System card expose the top three compute owners. The canonical morning-after browser regression covers 1h/4h/24h plus reload, focused control/range regressions passed 5/5, all 15 Node shards passed, and the final eight-lane gate passed in 401.89s. Restarted 8881 is the sole priority-100 owner with protocol 20/schema 3 and every sampler family at zero failures/missed/late cycles; its 60-second web-process measurement improved from the old 25.22% average to 0.87% average (1.9% p95, 11.4% max). The live 24h binary response was 2.06 MB with 147 main + 147 token records, six coverage intervals, and 128 bounded epochs.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.research-agent-status-continuous-lines.md`, `DOIT.yostats-local-services-table-layout.md`, and `DOIT.yostats-logs-tab-and-libproc-fallback-warning.md`. Agent-status held rosters now remain continuous only across an asynchronous refresh; real interior/trailing sampler loss is an honest no-data overlay. System -> Local services is a stable transposed table with aligned non-wrapping labels, wrapping Queues, and narrow horizontal scrolling. The Logs sub-tab merges bounded leveled diagnostics and exposes a deduplicated warning whenever native libproc/procfs discovery falls back to bounded cached `lsof`. The focused status, System, and Logs browser regressions plus the non-blocking stats sampler test passed (4 tests), and `static_build.py --check` is clean.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.jsonl-preview-rendered-table.md` and `DOIT.jsonl-preview-space-and-stretch.md`. JSONL/NDJSON files now open as bounded heterogeneous tables in Preview while Edit remains raw source; malformed rows remain visible, nested values retain their full hover value, and extra rows/keys are explicitly bounded. The shared table fills its Preview container at any pane width: compact timestamp/type tracks remain bounded while payload takes remaining space and resizes with the pane, without a hard-coded viewport width. The current editor-preview layout shard passed all 15 suites, the focused JSONL Selenium test passed, and `static_build.py --check` is clean.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.https-self-signed-by-default.md`. Bare YOLOmux now serves generated self-signed HTTPS by default; a supplied `--cert`/`--key` pair takes precedence, `--http` is the explicit plain-HTTP path, and the legacy self-signed spellings remain compatible. Missing OpenSSL falls back loudly to HTTP with actionable guidance instead of preventing startup. README and startup messaging describe this default without the old enable-HTTPS nag. The exact-HEAD eight-lane gate passed, and the guarded 8881 restart confirmed one fresh HTTPS listener with the expected unauthenticated 401 health response.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.finder-sync-star-all-touched-paths.md`. Finder Sync's `★` now marks every directory touched by the selected session, including its working-directory root and touched ancestors, while leaving expansion-only pass-through rows unstarred. Switching sessions replaces the marker set without stale stars. The shared Finder detail popover explains a starred row as `★ Modified by <selected session>`; ordinary rows get no extra detail line or request. Focused Finder Selenium coverage exercises the real shared hover controller and the root/non-root, multi-path, session-switch, pass-through, and collapse contracts. The final canonical eight-lane gate passed in 417.43 seconds after one unrelated load-sensitive pricing-worker timing outlier passed alone in 1.04 seconds.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.rebuild-stats-token-db-from-jsonl.md`. The new offline rebuild tool discovers Claude/Codex transcript families, reuses the production atom parser/projector, deduplicates stable usage identities, and replaces only token/cost components while preserving live metrics and output-only lower-bound buckets. Apply is fail-closed: it detects/stops shared-state servers only when explicitly requested, disables supervised respawn for the operation, verifies no live socket/owner/DB opener, holds the registry and daemon locks, creates a timestamped SQLite backup, and commits the rebuild in one transaction. The real 2026-07-12 apply rebuilt 1,205 retained buckets from 407 families/718 files and 1,012,201 stable atoms, preserved 5,431 live-metric buckets and 522 selected transcriptless output-only buckets, removed 97 duplicate identities, and reported zero truncation and zero `billable < output`; backup `stats-history.sqlite3.backup-20260712T221618Z` passed integrity checks. Focused rebuild tests passed 6/6, the exact-HEAD canonical eight-lane gate passed in 429.83 seconds, and 8881 restarted with one listener and one statsd owner returning the expected unauthenticated 401.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.finder-sync-root-home-memory-star.md`. Finder Sync now roots home-contained worktrees at the home tree, displays that root as `~`, expands the full ancestor chain to the synced working directory, keeps per-session expansion/manual-collapse memory even when multiple tabs share the same home root, and never lets sync auto-expansion reopen a user-collapsed path. The deepest synced affected working directory row now shows a localized bright `★` marker that follows the selected session; manually collapsed starred rows stay collapsed while keeping the marker.
- Verification: `python3 tools/static_build.py --check`, `node tests/layout_url.test.js --shard editor_preview`, `node tests/layout_url.test.js --shard layout_async`, focused Finder Selenium coverage for root/full-chain/star/manual-collapse/per-session memory, and the full `python3 tools/check.py` gate passed in 454.30 seconds. Port 8881 restarted as primary with one listener PID 84407, `YOLOMUX_BACKGROUND_OWNER_PRIMARY_PORT=8881`, and `/api/ping` returned the expected auth-gated 401.

- Completed and removed the 2026-07-12 Finder/YO!stats/mobile/upload service queues. Finder Sync now roots every home-contained tmux or file sync at `~`, carries the focused cwd into affected dirs even when session-files only reports repo roots, expands the full ancestor chain without crawling unrelated home siblings, preserves per-session same-root expansion/manual-collapse memory, and threads explicit child expansions as user-owned reads so client-push background suppression cannot mark a plan applied while hiding the working dir. Finder/Differ/Tabber date text now resolves against each row's owning surface, so Finder Ago and Differ Date/None no longer drift. YO!stats history readiness treats missing/malformed `history.coverage` as a bounded error with Retry and centers loading/error overlays in the visible scrollport. YO!stats System -> Local services is a transposed, in-place-updated live table with Started/Last ran, fresh/stale/prev value state, and Queues last. macOS image paste no longer forces transcript/session rescans or agent discovery on the upload path; Darwin cwd/transcript discovery uses bounded libproc/lsof paths where it still runs. Focused verification passed Node layout (15 shards), `tests/test_browser_finder.py` (21), YO!stats/browser focused checks, upload/session backend tests, static build/check, and the final closeout gate/restart recorded in the handoff.

- Completed and removed the mobile terminal keyboard queues. The smart keyboard now has `Tab`, `^B`/tmux prefix, and overflow on the top row; `Esc`, `Ctrl`, `Shift`, `Alt`, `Cmd`, and `^C` in the left vertical modifier column; copy/paste beside the cursor cluster; and a palette drag model where dragging the open palette moves the attached launcher/`×` and both remain pane-clamped. The mini keyboard remains non-highlightable. Focused verification passed static build/check plus Node/browser smart-keyboard regressions.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.movable-keyboard-launcher.md`. The touch terminal smart-keyboard control is now a movable per-session launcher: the launcher stores its own pane-clamped position, toggles to `×` while open, owns tap/drag/long-press separation without a second palette close/drag handle, and keeps the palette edge-aware inside the same terminal pane. Read-only/coarse-pointer/share gating remains unchanged: desktop-pointer viewers get no launcher, read-only coarse-pointer views can move the launcher while mutating keys remain disabled. The GUI spec and coverage map name the source and browser owners. Focused verification passed the generated-bundle live launcher drag/toggle regression, the existing touch smart-keyboard browser regression, the read-only/coarse-pointer Node assertions, static build checks, and the canonical eight-lane gate in 343.01 seconds.

- Hardened `boot.sh`, `yolo-dev-start`, background ownership, and the local check runner after overlapping restarts multiplied transcript/repository warmups and repeated test runs overloaded a Mac. Both launchers now share one per-user start lock and an 8-CPU-capped slow-ramp gate before asset, agent, launchd, tmux, or server mutation; macOS servers are resubmitted as one supervised LaunchAgent each. A preferred primary starts first and remains owner without breaking follower failover, every row proves stable ownership and an empty refresh queue, and startup discovery uses read-only tmux existence checks rather than forced transcript rebuilds. Expensive checks share a per-user fail-fast lock; `--serial` omits xdist entirely. macOS test lanes use a conservative 50% of the capped CPU budget (2/1/1 workers), while Linux retains 75%. Focused ownership/startup/service/check verification passed 138 tests plus 22 sequencing/lock tests. Loaded Mac QA exposed and repaired eight stale/timing-sensitive browser contracts plus one warm-cache assertion; the final canonical eight-lane gate passed in 334.52 seconds, including 2,126 non-browser tests, 3 boot tests, 429 browser tests with 5 expected skips, E2E, and all 15 Node shards. The final real macOS ramp started 8882/8880/8881/8883 one at a time as four `runs=1` LaunchAgents at one shared SHA: 8882 stayed priority-100 owner with one acquisition and zero releases, every follower had zero acquisitions/releases, every queue stayed empty, read-only discovery found all five tmux sessions, and load fell from 5.61/11.24 to 3.78/10.26 during the ramp.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.cost_summary.md`. YO!stats now retains provider-neutral billable usage atoms alongside its compatible output-token activity projection, with exact model/effort/profile/tier, cache role, modality/unit, root/subagent/tool/source identity, and explicit telemetry completeness. A local packaged pricing seed and secure SQLite catalog provide effective-dated API list-price evidence; bounded, reviewed OpenAI/Anthropic/Google refreshes activate together, while OpenRouter/LiteLLM corroborate only. The Cost summary directly follows Model tokens/min and consumes the same displayed range, showing a compact Input/Cache/Output/Total card and a safe accessible detail popover with token-class, model, and source reconciliation. Exact estimates use `est. $…`; unpriced, opaque, incomplete, or legacy data remains `est. ≥$…` or `est. —`. Retained transcript history has byte high-water replay, staged source replacement, and catalog reprojection. Focused verification passed pricing (23), statsd (39), Node layout (15 shards), and the live Chrome cost-summary browser regression; port 8882 restarted with expected unauthenticated 401.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.multiprocess_background_work.md`. YOLOmux now keeps each `yolomux.py` port as the latency-critical HTTP/WebSocket control plane while shared local services own heavy or stateful work: `statsd` is the YO!stats SQLite/encoding writer, existing `indexd` remains the Quick Open SQLite owner, `jobd` brokers bounded stateless CPU work, and `approvald` owns target-keyed auto-approval. The checked parent is `yolomux_lib.local_services`, which now owns versioned RPC framing, restrictive Unix-socket creation, singleton lifecycle, common diagnostics, foreground entry points, package launch behavior, and shared service clients; the final runtime fix creates sockets under a restrictive bind-time umask before the `0600` chmod so no transient `0755` socket is exposed, and metadata warmers stop before their no-network comparison after owner demotion. Negative searches for retired stats writers/encoders remain absent from product code, with only guard strings in `tests/test_common.py`; tracked pre-archive diff evidence was 94 files changed, 6509 insertions, and 4874 deletions. Focused verification passed `python3 -m pytest tests/test_local_services_rpc.py -q` (13 passed), `python3 -m pytest tests/test_background_owner.py -q` (51 passed), `python3 -m pytest tests -n auto -m 'not node_bridge and not e2e and not browser' -q` (2043 passed), and the final canonical `python3 tools/check.py` gate passed in 92.14 seconds. Port 7771 restarted from this checkout as PID 3369960 with `/api/ping` returning the expected unauthenticated 401 in 45ms.

- Quick Open now treats Cmd-P as a file-only chooser, so `FILE ACTIONS`, tabs, and settings cannot crowd out an exact filename such as `t5t.md`; Shift-Cmd-P remains the mixed command/pane search. The persistent indexer no longer lets a losing lock contender unlink the active Unix socket. Read-only web servers now route a cold, unavailable on-disk index query to the indexer's ready in-memory snapshot rather than falling back to a capped walk that can return fuzzy noise and miss an exact file. A capped cold walk reports warming with no false results. Regressions cover the competing indexer socket, indexer-served search protocol, read-only handoff, capped fallback, Cmd-P result domain, and the existing palette consumers updated to their correct surfaces. The live 7773 indexer returned `notes/t5t/t5t.md` as the first `t5t.md` result; port 7773 was restarted and returned the expected unauthenticated 401. The canonical eight-lane gate passed in 75.08 seconds.

- Completed normalized YO!info work-graph migration. The old singular `session.project` model could enrich only one ranked repository, which hid active work in other TmuxPanes; historical transcript paths had no explicit graph edge, so they could disappear or be attributed ambiguously; and linked worktrees could suppress the shared repository's available branches. Session metadata now exposes one versioned graph from `TmuxSession` through `TmuxWindow`, `TmuxPane`, `RuntimeActor`, and `PathObservation` to `GitWorktree`, `LocalGitRepository`, `LocalBranch`, and `PullRequest`. Every observed repository and historical path remains attributable, linked worktrees share one complete branch inventory while retaining their own checkout and dirty state, and tabs, YO!info, Finder/Differ, Tabber, the Info Bar, menus, notifications, and YO!share all select only through shared graph selectors. The retired `session.project` and `window_metadata[].git` owners are absent from the API and guarded against reintroduction. The final cache-race fix makes a GitHub-warmed graph publish one deferred metadata refresh when its content changes, without looping on the graph generation token; this is why a first load now gains Session 3's PR #80 rather than waiting for an unrelated refresh. Focused verification passed the cache-race regressions, live Session 3 branch/PR validation (15 current frontend-crates3 branches and open draft PR #80), and the final eight-lane gate in 94.86 seconds; the active 7771 backend was restarted and returned its expected 401 login gate.

- Finder can now manage Quick Open exclusions in place. Right-clicking any file or directory covered by an indexed root offers `Exclude from index`; right-clicking that exact exclusion offers `Include in index`, while root index/unindex behavior remains intact, unrelated files cannot become index roots, and descendants cannot override an excluded ancestor. Settings reconciliation repaints visible rows and refreshes the affected root, and exact rows say `indexed` or `index excluded` immediately before Date/Ago in a status slot sized for the full phrase rather than the old `I`. Selected labels now consume the selected-row foreground token and pass measured dark/light contrast instead of retaining the generic badge's dark text. A restored down-pointing directory whose children have not rendered is explicitly loading and shows the shared 900ms spinner until its listing arrives. All 39 Layout Async, 17 Share/theme, 63 Layout Restore, Editor, and focused browser contracts passed. Loaded parallel gates encountered unrelated stats/SQLite timing outliers; the unchanged tests passed five and three isolated repetitions respectively, and the final canonical eight-lane gate passed in 54.45 seconds.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.macos_test_portability.md`. Two macOS failures exposed real Quick Open bugs: fuzzy matching could borrow characters from the absolute root prefix to return unrelated files, and an index directory nested below its indexed root could ingest its own SQLite, manifest, and lock files. Search now matches only filenames and paths relative to the selected root, while full and incremental index builds share one internal-storage exclusion with cache-signature invalidation only for affected roots. The remaining failures were portable-test defects: tmux fixtures now use one secure, unique, short `/tmp` socket path compatible with Darwin's Unix-domain socket limit, and boot-script tests exercise arbitrary configured ports plus either supported tmux-environment cleanup mechanism without branching on the host OS. `YOLOMUX_PORT` now defines the arbitrary primary port as well as the default, so it retains non-dev behavior instead of being compared with a platform-specific number. Live restart verification found and fixed one additional real lifecycle bug: a port-bind failure could call `server_close()` before subclass fields existed, masking `EADDRINUSE` with an `AttributeError`; the cleanup path now tolerates partial initialization and has a real socket-collision regression. Focused verification passed all 24 file-index tests, 50 background-owner/search tests, the ten affected tmux tests, all four boot-script tests, and the bind-failure lifecycle tests; the final canonical eight-lane gate passed in 56.08 seconds. On this Mac, port 8880 was returned to its loaded `KeepAlive` LaunchAgent after diagnosing a conflicting manually detached copy; launchd PID 67737 remained stable across three probes, returned the expected unauthenticated 401, and produced no further bind retries or errors.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.side-panes.md`. Pane role and edge position are now explicit, independent state: Generic Panes inherit the shared pane contract, while `side:left|right` specializes it with outer-edge canonicalization, intrinsic tabs, minimize-only chrome, width preservation, and a one-third viewport cap. Finder/Differ/Tabber are Side-required on wide layouts; YO!* tabs may be created in either role but remain role-sticky; terminals and other ordinary tabs remain Generic, including when moved to the far-right edge. Constrained layouts use one Generic Pane, and returning wide restores the triplet to a left Side Pane without pulling YO!* tabs across roles. URL/share/Dockview serialization, legacy migration, drop/move/split/swap/fill/layout-mode capability checks, fallback/Dockview DOM role data, responsive transitions, malformed-layout repair, and generic fillers all use the same registry and classifiers. Intentional empty panes now survive Dockview adoption and responsive normalization, generic serialized split percentages no longer inherit retired Finder-width heuristics, and topbar packing now starts from the full presentation on every measurement so expansion and contraction produce the same result. Validation passed 21 Side Pane unit cases, all 15 Node shards, focused responsive/role/chrome/geometry browser tests, five repeated topbar resize tests, and the canonical eight-lane gate in 71.61 seconds with 403 browser tests passing and four expected local golden baselines refreshed after visual review. ## 2026-06-29

### macOS Codex transcript detection and YO!stats token history

- Completed macOS Codex transcript detection. Darwin now uses bounded `lsof` lookups for the process cwd and open rollout file, while Linux keeps the `/proc` path. Cwd fallback selects the newest-mtime matching rollout, fixing resumed Codex sessions whose old rollout filename continues receiving new output. The rollout lookup is cached for 15 seconds with a one-second `lsof` timeout.
- Added a dedicated server-aggregated Agent tokens/min history for wide graph ranges: two-minute points for 4–8 hours and five-minute points for 16–24 hours. Client latency, API/SSE, bandwidth, and narrow token views keep their existing data paths.
- Verified a live macOS `7777:%0` Codex agent resolves to the exact `lsof` rollout and reports 223991 generated tokens. Rebuilt static assets, restarted `bash boot.sh 7777`, confirmed it listens on `7777`, and `/api/ping` returns the expected auth-gated `401`. Focused Python tests (375), browser layout tests (132), static check, diff check, and the repository check gate pass.

## 2026-06-24

### Background indexing owner visibility

- The client tracks whether the current browser is connected to the `search-index` owner and `stats-sampler` owner through `/api/background/status`, but YO!info no longer renders that server-role strip. The top-right ownership chip shows the compact `IDX|STATS|SESS: leader/follower` state for shared background jobs and refreshes on click, manual refresh, EventSource reconnect, and `background_owner_changed`. Runtime owner takeovers now notify the app through a background-owner acquire callback, so a follower that takes over after a dead indexing owner publishes `background_owner_changed` instead of silently changing only the on-disk owner record. `docs/DEVELOPMENT.md` now spells out the `YOLOMUX_STATE_DIR` layout: `background-owner/`, `search_index/`, `watch-index.json`, and separate per-target auto-approve locks under `locks/`.

### Filesystem watch diff/keyframe frames

- Implemented MPEG-style filesystem watch frames. The server now records a bounded shared filesystem snapshot history, sends full frames for the first/keyframe/manual paths, sends compact `fs_changed` invalidations for ordinary watch changes, and answers stateless client `GET /api/fs/watch-diff?since=<token>` requests with changed-root diffs or a full stale-token fallback. Browser clients keep their own token, request `full=1` from the top-right refresh path, invalidate removed roots, and no per-client server state is needed for multiple clients per server. Verification: focused filesystem watch and route tests, `node tests/layout_async.test.js`, and full `python3 tools/check.py`.

### Visual animation verification rule

- Refactored the agent-status ball debugging lesson into one readable source of truth. `docs/specs/GUI.md` owns the detailed visual contract and status-ball acceptance criteria; `docs/DEVELOPMENT.md` now keeps only the workflow checklist; `AGENTS.md` points agents back to those docs instead of repeating the full rule. The root lesson is still the same: prove the exact reported element changes in the browser over time before saying a visual animation fix is done.

### Differ rootless-empty session-files flicker

- Fixed the Differ panel flashing between `~/yolomux.dev8002` and an empty result for Tab `8002`. The frontend accepted a transient `session_files_ready` payload with `repos: []` and `files: []` for the selected session, so a weak session-discovery snapshot could blank an already-loaded rooted Differ payload until the next rooted payload arrived. Background fetches and SSE pushes now preserve the current same-session Differ payload when the incoming update is rootless and empty; a real clean result still applies because it carries the live repo root with `count: 0`. Added regression coverage for the exact `8002` / `~/yolomux.dev8002` shape and rebuilt `static/yolomux.js`. Focused verification: `node tests/share_theme.test.js` and `python3 -m pytest tests/test_node_suite.py`.

### Tmux signal patch key refactor

- Completed and removed `DOIT.refactor_tmux_signal_keys.md`. Tmux signal window patching now routes record keys through one backend helper (`window_record_key()`, backed by `window_key()`) and one frontend helper (`tmuxSignalWindowKey()`), instead of rebuilding `session:window_index` in `app.py`, patch merge code, pane lookup, and global activity counters. Added regression coverage for fallback session/window records with no explicit `key`.

### Slow API/SSE payload optimization

- Completed and removed `DOIT.optimize_slow_api_calls.md`. Auto-approve roster status now has a single cached stale-while-refresh owner with single-flight refreshes; session-scoped auto-approve calls bypass the full roster cache; timer `auto_approve_changed` pushes compact `{refresh: true, signature}` invalidations instead of the all-session roster; auto-approve window rows skip path/git inventory and reuse selected-pane screen classification; Debug shows auto-approve phase timings. Client-event payloads are smaller: `fs_changed` sends compact refresh invalidations, watch-state transcript pushes send signature-only refreshes, unchanged session-files payloads do not republish across repeated `fs_changed` triggers, watch-root registration is debounced, and tmux signal pushes use changed-window patches with full-payload fallback. Startup control-socket `BrokenPipeError` is treated as a benign disconnect. Verification: focused `python3 -m pytest` slices for auto-approve/control/client-event paths, `python3 -m pytest tests/test_app.py -k 'auto_approve_payload_includes_agent_window_statuses' -q`, `python3 tools/static_build.py --check`, and `node tests/layout_async.test.js`.

### YO!agent oversized conversation recovery

- Completed and removed `DOIT.yoagent_chat_413_request_entity_too_large.md`. YO!agent now caps persisted auxiliary/tool stream data through one shared sanitizer for conversation JSONL and live stream state, so megabyte `rg`/tool output lines cannot wedge future turns. Codex app-server sends detect HTTP 413 / request-too-large failures, drop the poisoned resume thread, start a fresh Codex thread, and retry once before surfacing an actionable error. The YO!agent chat UI now shows a specific “conversation too large to resume” message instead of raw `chat failed: Request Entity Too Large`, and the YO!agent prompt now tells the model to keep shell output bounded with `rg -M 2000 --max-columns 2000`, targeted paths, and summaries. Verification: `python3 -m pytest tests/test_yoagent_stream_state.py tests/test_yoagent_transports.py tests/test_activity_summary.py -q`, `python3 -m pytest tests/test_app.py -k 'reset_yoagent_chat_clears_cli_sessions or yoagent_codex_backend_falls_back_to_exec_when_app_server_fails' -q`, `python3 -m pytest tests/test_app.py -k 'yoagent_model_chat_appends_history_and_skips_activity_for_simple_followup' -q`, `python3 tools/static_build.py`, and `node tests/layout_async.test.js`.

### Slow fresh reload and activity refresh

- Completed and removed `DOIT.yolomux-slow-reload-fix.md`. Fresh reload slowness had two separate causes: large versioned static startup assets were served raw with `Cache-Control: no-store`, and all-session activity summary repeatedly scanned the 48 MB event log once per session. Static GET/HEAD now negotiates gzip for compressible assets, sends `Vary: Accept-Encoding`, and gives only `?v=` URLs immutable cache headers while HTML/JSON remain `no-store`; live 8003 gzip checks shrank `yolomux.js` 2,088,364->479,661 bytes, `yolomux.css` 416,024->75,068 bytes, Dockview 794,201->136,607 bytes, and xterm 392,419->91,653 bytes. `EventLog.tail()` now scans backward and `tail_many()` lets activity summary collect recent events for all sessions in one pass; live 8003 timings after restart were activity summary 2.297s, forced activity summary 4.195s, cached transcripts 0.004s, and forced transcripts 0.753s. Frontend boot now paints the saved shell before awaiting transcript metadata, with `static/yolomux.js` rebuilt from `static_src`. Verification: `python3 -m pytest tests/test_server_static.py -q`, `python3 -m pytest tests/test_observability.py -q`, `python3 -m pytest tests/test_app.py -k activity_summary_payload -q`, `python3 -m pytest tests/test_static_build.py::test_generated_static_assets_are_current -q`, `python3 tools/static_build.py --check`, `node tests/share_theme.test.js`, `python3 -m py_compile yolomux.py tmux_wall.py auto_approve_tmux.py yolomux_lib/*.py`, authenticated live 8003 timing/header probe, and 8003 restart/ping from `/home/keivenc/yolomux.dev8003`.
- Follow-up queue replay added explicit timing regression coverage for the reload fix: `test_event_log_tail_timing_regression_stops_before_old_history` makes old log history artificially slow so a full forward scan fails, and `test_activity_summary_payload_batches_recent_events_for_multiple_sessions` proves activity summary batches recent events through one `tail_many()` call. Re-measured live 8003 after restart: activity summary 5.036s, forced activity summary 4.615s, cached transcripts 0.009s, forced transcripts 1.644s; static gzip remained correct (`yolomux.js` 2,088,568->479,713 bytes, `yolomux.css` 416,024->75,068 bytes, Dockview 794,201->136,607 bytes, xterm 392,419->91,653 bytes). `cProfile` showed the old event-log scan is no longer the hot path; remaining activity-summary time is metadata/session-files/background work, now routed to the active single-owner background-indexing queue.
- Drained and removed `DOIT.slow-fresh-reload-timing-regression.md` after moving it from `/tmp`; its only remaining unchecked follow-up was already represented by `DOIT.single_owner_background_indexing.md`.

- Final design (after iterating through a symbol opacity-pulse and a symbol<->ball alternate, both of which the user rejected): every Claude/Codex status indicator shows its agent symbol STATIC with a SEPARATE glowing ball beside it — `[symbol][ball]`, side by side — on dock pane tabs, the tmux sub-window bar, Tabber rows, and Info Pane buttons. #### YO!agent persisted-job watch predicates
- Shipped the first batch of the persisted-job watch roadmap: `notify_session_needs_input` fires only on real `needs-input`/question states, `notify_session_blocked` fires on approval/error/disconnect blockers, `notify_session_done_after_working` fires only after that job first observed `working` and later observed an accepting/done/idle state, and `cancel_session_jobs` cancels queued or pending-confirmation jobs for one session while leaving fired/failed/timed-out and other-session jobs alone. YO!agent chat now understands phrases such as `notify me when session 1 asks a question`, `tell me when agent 1 is blocked`, `notify me when session 1 is done after it was working`, and `cancel pending jobs for session 1`; the direct API also exposes `POST /api/yoagent/jobs/cancel-session`.

- Completed and removed `DOIT.done_autoapprove_mock_agents.md`: mock Claude/Codex yes/no approval handling is verified through detector and real-tmux mock E2E coverage; the file had no active unchecked boxes, only non-blocking cursor-placement polish noted as `[~]`.
- Verification: the latest `python3 tools/check.py` passed all 7 lanes (`CHECK PASSED in 42.84s`); the archived files' audits name the existing focused tests for warning demotion, backend diagnostics, and mock-agent approval.

#### Self-update restart and browser reload UX
- Completed and removed `DOIT.self_update_restart_and_ux.md`. Self-update now records a restart context for the running checkout, resolves script/module launchers, preserves argv/env needed for the active server, relaunches from `PROJECT_ROOT` with a detached helper that kills only its own PID, and documents the launcher-agnostic contract. The browser side dismisses the update toast immediately, hides the badge, starts self-update-specific ping polling after `restarting: true`, reloads when safe, suppresses the generic reload banner for the owned target, and defers with a clear Software Update toast when dirty editors or active typing would be interrupted.
- Verification: pytest covers relative script, absolute script, module launcher, stripped-env/nohup-style env, current-PID-only kill, helper detachment/stdio/log behavior, and no systemd/pkill; node tests cover immediate toast removal, reload polling, banner suppression, dirty-editor deferral, and active-typing deferral; full `python3 tools/check.py` passed all 7 lanes (`CHECK PASSED in 40.25s`).

## 2026-06-17

### Tmux, Terminal, YO!share, and Tabber

#### Real repo inferred from agent-edited dirs in session metadata
- A Claude/Codex launched from `$HOME` (or any other non-repo cwd) no longer shows "no git checkout detected" while it is actually editing files in a real repo. `candidate_session_cwds` now also feeds `session_touched_dirs(info)` — the directories each agent has EDITED files in, from the same transcript edit-tool scan the Modified-files/Tabber panes use (edits, not reads) — so `session_git_inventory` and the YO!info repo list surface the real repo and branch even when the live pane cwd has no git checkout. The touched-dir signal outranks the session-number default; final primary selection across all candidates still happens by git activity in `repo_summary`.
- Added a `(path, mtime, size)` memoization cache to `scan_claude_transcript` (matching the existing codex scanner) since `candidate_session_cwds` now scans transcripts on the hot metadata-refresh path and an unchanged transcript should read from disk once.
- Tests: `test_candidate_session_cwds_surfaces_transcript_touched_repo` (home pane editing a real repo -> repo detected), `test_session_touched_dirs_collects_edited_dirs` (dir dedup, reads excluded), `test_scan_claude_transcript_refreshes_cache_on_change` (no stale cache hit after append). Reproduced live against the real session 8003 transcript (home pane -> `~/yolomux.dev8003` branch surfaced). Commit `a874f13`.

#### Full-speed wheel scroll for alt-screen panes (claude/codex/vim)
- The terminal wheel was unconditionally routed into tmux copy-mode, which scrolls nothing on alt-screen TUIs (they own the mouse and keep no scrollback, `history_size` stays 0), so the app never received the wheel. Gated the copy-mode route on `sessionPaneIsAlternateScreen`; alt-screen panes forward the wheel to the app, driven by the same `terminalWheelSignedLines` count the copy-mode path uses (plus a per-session fractional remainder for touchpads) so alt-screen scroll matches scrollback-pane speed. Layout-suite regression `t@6318` + a `docs/specs/TMUX.md` "wheel routing by screen mode" note. Commit `ddf3bc7`.

#### tmux / share / auto-approve lifecycle hardening
- A batch of verified backend/frontend lifecycle and race fixes: share `viewer_ids` iterated without the lock (now a deep-copy snapshot), PTY resize dropped while a tab is hidden and never re-sent on return, openpty fd / viewer-registration leak when attach setup raises before the try, untimed tmux subprocess calls under the share upstream lock, `reader_loop` master_fd use-after-close race, auto-approve worker leak when the watched session dies outside YOLOmux, codex summary per-chunk UTF-8 split and strict capture-pane decode, SIGKILL with no wait leaving a transient zombie, share send with no socket timeout, write-after-dispose terminal race, uncancelled fit timers on teardown, and a non-ASCII WebSocket key returning 400 instead of 500. Restored the diff-overview no-temporary-rail invariant and rebuilt its browser test on a frozen single-chunk fixture instead of the moving `docs/TODO.md`. Guards: `t@7185` + ~12 python tests (viewer_ids snapshot, hidden-tab pending resize, bounded timeouts, sigkill wait, openpty cleanup, codex UTF-8 across chunks, non-ASCII WS key, ...). Commit `1a2dfe7`.

#### tmux resize authority bound to the active browser
- Fixed the "pane too wide / expands to the widest screen" bug. Two browser surfaces on one session attach as two differently-sized tmux clients, and plain `window-size largest` let a wider background browser stretch the foreground pane. Now every YOLOmux attach starts with tmux `ignore-size`; when a Chrome/Safari page becomes active it scans its visible pane tabs, sends foreground resize claims for each visible xterm, clears `ignore-size` for those clients, and sets `ignore-size` on the other YOLOmux-managed clients for that session; re-entering an already-authoritative browser at the same dims is a tmux/PTY no-op. Guards: `test_configure_session_tmux_options_uses_active_surface_authority`, `test_claim_tmux_resize_authority_ignores_other_yolomux_clients`, plus node source-guards; `docs/specs/TMUX.md` and `GUI.md` document the contract. Commit `6e425c3`.

### Editor, Finder, Differ, and Files

#### Diff/Differ view: wrapped continuation rows of long added/changed lines no longer render blank (DOIT.2)
- In the `@codemirror/merge` diff view with word-wrap on, a long inserted/changed line that soft-wrapped showed only its first visual row — the continuation rows rendered blank (text was in the DOM but painted over). Root cause: the full-bleed green/red change band (`box-shadow: -100vw 0 0 …` + `clip-path: inset(0 -100vw)`) was applied to the INLINE `cm-insertedLine`/`cm-deletedLine` marks, not only the block lines; on a soft-wrapped inline mark that clip buries every continuation row under the parent `.cm-changedLine` block's band. Fix in `static_src/css/yolomux/60_editor_file_panels.css`: keep the band trick on block-level elements only (`.cm-changedLine`, `.cm-deletedChunk`, `.cm-insertedChunk`, `.cm-inlineChangedLine`) and reset `box-shadow: none; clip-path: none` on the inline marks — the block still paints the full-width fill so the band is unchanged and the buried text returns. No JS change. The "Expand / collapse all unchanged lines" control was never floating (`position: static`, zero overlap); it only looked wrong because the rows were blank.
- Regression: Selenium `tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_diff_wrapped_inserted_line_continuation_rows_show_text` asserts each wrapped continuation row has height > 0, non-empty caret text, and the inserted mark as the topmost painted element (word-wrap on + `collapseUnchanged` active) — verified it FAILS on the old CSS and passes on the fix; plus a `tests/layout_url.test.js` CSS-contract guard. Contract documented in `docs/specs/EDITOR-CODEMIRROR.md` and `docs/specs/GUI.md`. DOIT.2 queued and fully drained.

### Build, Refactor, Docs, and Tests

#### Gate speedup: stop double-running the node suite
- The default `tools/check.py` gate ran the node layout suite twice concurrently — once as the always-on `node-layout` lane and again inside the `pytest` lane via `test_node_suite.py` (marker `node_bridge`), which shells out to the identical `node tests/layout_url.test.js`. It was the single slowest pytest item (~32s under load) and the two node processes thrashed the cores the 32 xdist browser workers needed. Excluded it from the default pytest lane with `-m "not node_bridge"` (node coverage stays via the `node-layout` lane; a bare `python3 -m pytest tests` still runs the bridge) and updated the `test_check_runner.py` guard. Full gate wall-clock dropped from ~47s to ~33s, verified green across 8 consecutive runs. Tuning `-n` did not help — the gate is bound by its single longest test. `docs/DEVELOPMENT.md` and `AGENTS.md` updated. Commit `dbfd981`.

#### Portable self-update restart
- Self-update restart no longer depends on `systemd-run`/`systemctl`/`pkill` (non-portable on macOS/non-systemd Linux, and the server failed to come back). It now spawns a detached `nohup bash -lc` helper that does a best-effort `kill`, waits 2s, a best-effort `kill -9`, then relaunches the same Python argv. Guard `test_self_update_restart_uses_portable_nohup_helper` asserts the portable `nohup bash -lc` shape and that `systemd-run`/`systemctl`/`pkill`/`setsid` are absent. Commit `f9e5758`.

### Editor, Finder, Differ, and Files

#### DOIT.78 deterministic image input into terminal-backed agent panes + test-gate integrity
- Completed and removed `DOIT.78.md`. Image paste/drop into a terminal pane now routes through ONE shared image-payload contract (`dataTransferHasImagePayload` + `dataTransferImageFiles` + `dataUrlToImageFile` in `99_terminal_boot.js`): any image-bearing exposure (File item, plain File list, image MIME type, rich `text/html` `<img>`, data: URL) is CLAIMED (`preventDefault`+`stopPropagation`) so the raw image can never leak to the agent as a rich `[Image #N]` attachment, then every image uploads and inserts only its text path reference. Multi-image is deterministic (N images → N refs). The file-drop path uses a new `hasUploadableDrag` (file OR image rich-data); the single-image `pastedImageFile` was removed in favor of the shared parent.
- Fixed a longstanding FALSE-GREEN in `tests/layout_url.test.js`: the trailing async IIFE silently hung on un-flushed batched `/api/fs/batch` listings (the harness stubbed `setTimeout` as a no-op, so the 8 ms fs-batch flush never fired), leaving `.finally` unreached and the process exiting 0 with NO `layout suite:` summary — masking every later test. Fixed structurally (the `setTimeout` shim now fires only the 8 ms fs-batch flush via real `setImmediate`; 8 ms is unique to it) + a real-node watchdog that fails loud (`SUITE DID NOT SETTLE`, exit 1) if the IIFE ever hangs again, and fixed the unmasked cross-realm `deepStrictEqual` defects (missing `canonical()`). Documented the whole failure mode in `AGENTS.md`.
- Tests: rich-data paste claim contract, multi-image paste→two-refs, a payload-matrix contract over the shared detector/extractor, and a source-grep invariant that paste/drop route through the shared parent. `node tests/layout_url.test.js`: `147 passed, 0 failed`.
- Verification: `python3 tools/static_build.py` rebuilt `static/yolomux.js`; full `python3 tools/check.py` was `909 passed, 1 failed` where the single failure is `test_readme_diff_waits_for_payload_before_building_codemirror`, a flaky CodeMirror merge-view Selenium `'Script error.'` UNRELATED to this change (no CodeMirror code touched) that passes on isolated re-run.

#### DOIT.74 terminal fit oscillation
- Completed and removed `DOIT.74.md`. Terminal fitting now uses one shared measurement contract: the pre-render fallback cell probe reads the bundled mono font token instead of a hardcoded fallback stack, local `fitTerminal` calls record a signature over content size, cell metrics, rows/cols, and terminal font settings, duplicate observer echoes skip before `term.resize()`, and Dockview host resize observer work is coalesced to one layout per animation frame.
- The existing bundled-font-ready refit remains the only post-font refit; no second font-ready path was added. The fit signature includes terminal font settings so real font/metric changes still refit, while identical geometry does not churn the xterm grid or remote tmux size.

Regression coverage lives in both `tests/layout_url.test.js` and `tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_terminal_fit_ignores_duplicate_resize_observer_echoes`, proving full-width cols, no duplicate resize on unchanged geometry, and resize on real width changes.

#### YO!share terminal buffer reset race
- Completed and removed `DOIT.share-terminal-buffer-reset.md`. Share-view terminals now track whether `/ws/share-view` has delivered bytes, skip `term.reset()` on later host-size fits after bytes have painted, and still resize/refresh to the host rows/cols. This fixes the case where a right-top pane could be DOM `mirrored` but visually blank because a delayed fit or `terminal-host-resize` cleared the xterm buffer after the tmux repaint.
- Replay health/debug now reports terminal stream state separately from DOM mirror state, including stream status, socket ready state, received-byte flag/count, last byte age, last reset age, and skipped reset count per terminal placeholder. The spec and test inventory now state that terminal content remains outside DOM replay and host resize must not clear already-painted viewer bytes.

#### YO!share Finder toggle replay drift
- Completed and removed `DOIT.share-finder-toggle-replay.md`. DOM replay keyframes/deltas now own a replay-only epoch/sequence, so interleaved semantic frames such as `ui-state`, `layout`, and Safari-cadence `geometry-digest` no longer make the next DOM delta look non-contiguous. Topology/keyframe publication drains pending mutation and terminal-placeholder batches so stale RAF-delayed deltas cannot cross a keyframe boundary.
- DOM delta payloads now carry terminal placeholder metadata and the viewer applies it after child-list mutations, so moved/recreated terminal panes rebind the same xterm/socket instead of going blank or opening duplicate sockets. Replay health/debug copy now includes sanitized `lastReplayError` details with expected and actual epoch/sequence/base fields.
- Strengthened the real generated-link Selenium matrix: it waits for the host terminal before creating the share, opens the real `/share/<id>` debug URL, exercises rapid Finder toggles, paused Finder toggles, and forced 2000 ms geometry-digest cadence, and asserts the viewer stays `mirrored`, dropped/keyframe-request counters do not increase during the loops, terminal placeholders stay connected, and no shared terminal session has duplicate live sockets.

### Tmux, Terminal, YO!share, and Tabber

#### YO!share tab-popover geometry replay
- Fixed a real replay geometry gap in tab hover popovers. The previous test only proved the popup appeared, and the first strengthened version compared the full rect and failed: host and viewer had the same `left/top`, but the viewer recomputed `width` from `36vw` against its own viewport, so the popup wrapped wider/taller. `positionPaneTabPopover` now serializes host-computed inline `left`, `top`, and `width`, and read-only replay keeps viewer-local hover popovers disabled.

#### YO!share replay stale-delta and popover regression follow-up
- Diagnosed the cursor jitter and occasional blank viewer as a replay repair loop: stale DOM deltas arriving after a newer keyframe were being classified as gaps, causing repeated `viewer behind` status and keyframe rebuilds. Fixed replay sequence handling so old/already-applied deltas increment `staleFrames` and are ignored, while true non-contiguous future deltas still request repair.
- Fixed the tab-hover info regression in replay clients. The corrected contract is host-owned popup mirroring: tab popover positions are serialized onto the replayed node, and read-only replay clients do not bind local hover controllers that could create client-only popup geometry.
- Added debug detail so future keyframe requests include the actual frame numbers (`epoch`, `sequence`, `baseSequence`, `currentEpoch`, `lastSequence`) instead of only `reason: gap`.
- Reflected the missed coverage in `AGENTS.md`, `docs/DEVELOPMENT.md`, and `docs/specs/SHARE_MIRRORING.md`: tests must cover stale-after-keyframe, true gap, replay listener rebinding, and debug/profiling fields. The old Selenium test missed the bug because it asserted the previous wrong behavior, that a stale epoch should request a keyframe.
- Verification: `python3 tools/static_build.py`, `node tests/layout_url.test.js`, focused Selenium `python3 -m pytest tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_share_replay_shell_applies_only_contiguous_deltas -q`, full `python3 tools/check.py` (`CHECK PASSED in 37.34s`), dev1 restart on port 8001, and HTTPS `/api/ping` returning unauthenticated `401`.

#### DOIT.72 YO!share DOM replay rewrite
- Completed and removed `DOIT.72.md`. YO!share read-only and write viewers now use the replay shell by default: the host serializes sanitized `#appRoot` keyframes and coalesced DOM/scroll/pointer deltas, viewers apply only contiguous epoch/sequence frames into inert DOM, and repair requests a fresh keyframe on join, gap, digest mismatch, unsafe mutation, slow-viewer backpressure, or manual debug. The temporary semantic escape hatch remains for diagnostics through `shareReplay=0`, `shareSemantic=1`, bootstrap `shareReplay: false`, or `localStorage.yolomux.shareReplaySemantic=1`.
- Terminal panes stay on the host-sized tmux byte stream. DOM replay carries terminal placeholders, viewer xterms bind/rebind to those placeholders without recreating the stream, `terminal-host-resize` resets rows/cols before the server requests a bounded `tmux refresh-client`, and terminal bytes keep flowing when replay falls behind.
- Write-mode shares now forward validated input intents instead of mutating local mirrored UI. HTTPS write viewers send terminal input/paste/scroll and allowed UI command intents over `/ws/share-ui`; the server rejects viewer-authored semantic `layout`, `ui-state`, Finder/editor, and `popup-layer` frames, so the host remains the only UI mutator and visual feedback returns through replay.
- Replay security and observability are covered by sanitizer/redaction helpers, keyframe/delta frame allowlists, a bounded delta ring, replay health diagnostics (`domDigest`, epoch/sequence, dropped frames, redaction policy, terminal placeholder health), and a build-time source guard that fails when private surfaces, token-bearing fields, terminal containers, or app-visible popup hosts bypass replay/redaction registration.
- Specs were moved under `docs/specs/`: `GUI.md`, `EDITOR-CODEMIRROR.md`, and `SHARE_MIRRORING.md`. README and `docs/DEVELOPMENT.md` now describe the replay default, terminal placeholders, write input-intent model, share sockets (`/ws/share-host`, `/ws/share-ui`, `/ws/share-view`), replay health, and the semantic escape hatch. During final validation, a banner regression was fixed so normal viewer-banner refreshes no longer overwrite replay `mirrored` status with the legacy `mirror ...` geometry placeholder.
- Verification: focused replay-health browser regression (`test_share_replay_debug_copy_exports_sanitized_health`), replay/source guards in `node tests/layout_url.test.js`, server protocol tests, the full `python3 tools/check.py` gate (`CHECK PASSED in 29.75s`), and dev1 restart/smoke on port 8001 with `/login` returning `200 0.044692`.

### Tmux, Terminal, YO!share, and Tabber

#### YO!share wrapped text/layout parity
- Fixed the recurring share-view indentation/wrap drift class by making the bundled UI/mono fonts block fallback-font layout, waiting for YOLOmux font metrics before the first app render, and remeasuring layout-sensitive surfaces after fonts settle. Wrapped text/control drift now reports as `textWraps`, so screenshot mismatches caused by local browser wrapping no longer hide behind `mirror ✓`.
- Follow-up fix: first render now waits for the actual font-ready promise instead of a 2.5s timeout race, so the host should not repaint/re-autosize a few seconds after load. Full UI-state snapshots also carry host wrapped-control metrics, and viewers apply host app-space width/height to native settings textareas before scroll replay; this keeps Preferences controls clipped/expanded exactly like the host instead of letting the viewer choose a different native textarea height.

#### YO!share resize repaint and mirrored chrome follow-up
- Fixed the post-layout terminal blanking race from the 2026-06-13 screenshots. When a share viewer reattaches to an existing shared terminal upstream, the server now requests a bounded `tmux refresh-client`; when the host terminal size changes, the server broadcasts `host-resize` before requesting the repaint so clients resize/reset before the fresh terminal bytes arrive instead of clearing the just-repainted buffer.
- Host layout commits now schedule a full UI-state snapshot after the layout frame, and the mirrored state now includes chrome that was previously browser-local: tab metadata visibility and the active YO!info/YO!agent sub-tab. Per-editor diff expand/collapse overrides now publish immediately, so expanding unchanged regions on the host updates read-only share clients without waiting for an unrelated snapshot.
- The no-regression plan is visual, not only source-grep: `tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_share_readonly_diff_scroll_and_popup_mirror_are_host_owned` renders a real CodeMirror diff in share view and asserts host-owned diff expansion, YO!agent sub-tab, tab metadata visibility, popup mirrors, and read-only scroll restoration. `tests/layout_url.test.js` covers the share snapshot/apply contract, and `tests/test_server_query.py` covers viewer reattach refresh plus resize/repaint ordering.

#### Mermaid Preview: split-view chopping, dark-on-dark labels, post-open jump, and bright-mode lines fixed
- Four live-reproduced Mermaid preview bugs (each verified against the running `:8003` server with real Dockview in authenticated headless Chrome, not synthetic fixtures, and each pinned by a regression that fails pre-fix):
- CHOPPING: in split view the diagram was chopped on the right at every zoom. Root cause (from dumping live geometry): the preview pane is `position:absolute; inset:0 0 0 50%` (right half), but `installPreviewZoomSurface` adds `.file-editor-preview-zoom-full { width:100%; height:100% }`, and an explicit `width:100%` overrides `right:0`, so the pane rendered full-width offset to `left:50%` and its right half ran off-screen. Fix: `.file-editor-content .file-editor-preview-pane-panel.file-editor-preview-zoom-full { width:auto; height:auto }` so the inset defines the box. Measured pane 930px -> 465px (the right half); diagram fully inside the visible half at Fit/1:1.
- DARK-ON-DARK LABELS: default (dark-fill) Mermaid nodes rendered dark text -> invisible (the "Open file" node and every node in classDef-less diagrams). Root cause: `svgReadableLabelColor` used the nearest ancestor fill (the label's own light fill) instead of the node's background shape, so it chose dark text for a dark node; and `svgStyleValue` failed to parse `fill:#fef3c7 !important` (Mermaid stamps `!important` on classDef fills), so light nodes read as fill-less. Fix: read the node's own background SHAPE fill (`svgNodeBackgroundFill`, skipping label-internal shapes) and strip a trailing `!important` in `svgStyleValue`. Measured: 0 unreadable labels, every node label now >=14:1 contrast vs its actual background.
- POST-OPEN JUMP: the diagram visibly shrank (~417->353px) ~150ms after appearing. Root cause: the editor pane opens at a transient height and Dockview re-lays-it-out (content 644->489px), so the fit-scaled diagram re-fit. Fix: a reveal gate keeps the diagram hidden (stage `visibility:hidden`, viewport still measurable) until its viewport size settles (debounced after the last change), then reveals once at the settled fit. Also coalesced the zoom resize observer to one apply per frame (the corrected half-width pane had surfaced a `ResizeObserver loop ... undelivered notifications` warning).
- BRIGHT-MODE LINES: in Bright/Vanilla preview (white surface) the diagram lines/labels were light-gray and illegible. Root cause: `mermaidPreviewConfig` and the edge/label colors read document `--text`, which follows the app theme (light when the app is dark) rather than the preview display mode. Fix: a `mermaidSurfacePalette()` keyed off `editorPreviewThemeState()` drives the config + edge + label colors, so Bright/Vanilla render dark lines/text on white and Dark renders light on dark; the diagram re-renders when the preview mode changes. Measured edge contrast 14.3:1 (dark) and 16.4:1 (Bright), up from ~1.1:1 illegible.
- Regression (`test_direct_mermaid_sample_real_bundle_keeps_svg_text_labels`, plus the markdown-visual mermaid test): asserts the split pane is ~half the content width and neither pane nor diagram overflows the content's right edge; asserts every node label clears 3:1 contrast against its node background (catches dark-on-dark, which the prior label-presence/font asserts missed); asserts the diagram reveals (not stuck hidden) after settle; toggles the preview to Bright/Vanilla and asserts the rendered edge stroke and node labels clear 3:1 against the white surface (catches the gray-on-white lines). `docs/specs/GUI.md` records the split-pane sizing, label-readability, preview-mode-palette, zoom-surface, and reveal-gate contracts. Full suite `python3 -m pytest tests -q` -> `629 passed`.

#### Previewer: type-aware Preview for images, SVG, PDF, Mermaid, structured data, and media
- Completed and removed `DOIT.previewer.md`, `DOIT.previewer.next.md`, and `DOIT.previewer.robust-inputs.md`. Preview capability and rendering kind route through one shared `PREVIEW_RENDERERS` registry + helper layer (`previewKindForPath` / `previewMediaKindForPath` / `previewMimeForPath` / `defaultFileEditorViewModeForPath`), not ad hoc extension checks. Direct PNG/JPG/JPEG/GIF/WebP/BMP/ICO/AVIF/SVG render as raw-file image previews; SVG goes through `<img src=/api/fs/raw>` and is never trusted as app DOM; PDF uses a sandboxed iframe with open/download fallback; `.mmd`/`.mermaid` default to Preview; audio/video use native controls (no autoplay); JSON/YAML/TOML/CSV/TSV and notebook `.ipynb` use bounded structured previews (notebook never executes code); misleading-extension binaries recover via sniffed MIME from `/api/fs/info`; unsupported binaries show path/MIME/size + open/download.
- Markdown Preview resolves local image URLs relative to the Markdown file's directory through `/api/fs/raw` (not the app URL), keeps safe external images, blocks unsafe sources, shows broken-image fallback UI, and has a local fallback parser when `marked`/highlight.js fail to load. Mermaid is local-vendored at `static/vendor/mermaid.min.js`, lazy-loaded, sanitized before display. Backend `read_raw` MIME handling covers AVIF/PDF/`.mmd`/`.mermaid`. `docs/specs/GUI.md` carries the durable preview contracts; `docs/preview-samples/` holds the sample files.

#### Preview zoom: shared zoom/pan surface + corner-case and refactor passes
- Completed and removed `DOIT.preview-zoom-refactor.md` and `DOIT.preview-zoom-corner-cases.md`. One owner for zoom policy/actions (`previewZoomPolicy`, `previewZoomActions`, `previewZoomStateForAction`) and renderer fit caps (`previewZoomRendererDefaults`, `previewZoomOptionsForKind`); image tabs moved off the legacy `imageMode` path onto the shared `previewZoom` surface; shared image checkerboard CSS. Corner cases fixed: split Preview no longer inherits full-Preview manual zoom (zoom keys scoped by preview/split/popout context), the pop-out zoom toolbar is hydrated rather than inert markup, pop-out CSS keeps the zoom-shell grid/scroll viewport, async pop-out snapshot replacement rehydrates zoom controls, and embedded Markdown Mermaid blocks use scoped zoom keys.

#### YO!share host-owned Finder and YO!info row state
- Fixed the client-only Finder jump where a read-only share viewer could briefly retarget or repaint Finder from local transcript/session-files refreshes after the host snapshot applied. Read-only share clients now treat Finder root, root mode, target session, and expansion as host-owned model state: local active-tab sync, local session-files payloads, active-file reveal, and manual opens no-op outside a host UI-state apply. Same-root host frames refresh in place instead of reopening the tree and briefly clearing expansion.
- Fixed the YO!info screenshot mismatch where a viewer rendered rows from its own scoped `transcriptMeta` instead of the host table. YO!info share snapshots now include sanitized branch-table rows, and read-only viewers render those host rows until a newer host row snapshot arrives.
- Completed the read-only share security audit in tests. Share-token POST auth now has a route matrix proving only `/api/fs/batch` is allowed; mutating POST routes including event, settings, share management, upload, tmux-window, watch roots, drop actions, YO!agent chat, and every fs mutation reject with 403. The allowed fs batch endpoint is pinned to list/info only, and the share UI websocket receive-only gate is asserted before JSON parsing or UI-state handling.
- Verification: `python3 tools/static_build.py`, `python3 tools/static_build.py --check`, `node tests/layout_url.test.js`, `python3 -m pytest -q tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_share_readonly_info_sort_and_horizontal_scroll_are_host_owned tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_share_readonly_finder_session_is_host_authoritative`, `python3 -m pytest -q tests/test_server_query.py`, and full `python3 tools/check.py` (`CHECK PASSED in 14.88s`).

#### YO!share YO!info columns, Differ TO ref, and remote cursor parity
- Fixed the YO!info mismatch where the host could resize the Branch/desc columns and horizontally scroll, but a share viewer kept its own default column widths, making the same host scroll offset reveal different columns. YO!info share snapshots now include resizable column widths; clients apply those widths without persisting or echo-publishing them, and the browser fixture asserts the applied CSS variables plus host-owned horizontal scroll restoration.
- Fixed Differ FROM/TO parity for repo-scoped refs. `setRepoDiffRefs()` now schedules a full share UI-state snapshot after updating the repo map, so selecting TO on the host no longer leaves read-only clients stuck on `current`.
- Changed the remote share cursor from a native-pointer-like marker to a colored target/crosshair. The target uses the existing participant color and stays inert above the mirrored app so it is visibly remote and cannot be confused with the local OS cursor.
- Audited adjacent share-state paths and kept coverage on the existing host-owned mirror contract: YO!info sort/scroll/columns, Differ refs, popup/menu/tab hover mirroring, editor diff expansion, viewport/appearance, terminal dimensions, and read-only scroll blocking. #### YO!share editor cursor stability
- Diagnosed the shared-editor cursor jump as stale CodeMirror view-state in full YO!share UI snapshots: typing changed the document and visible cursor, but the cached `editor.modes[].viewState` stayed at an older anchor such as the top of the file until a scroll or pane switch refreshed it. CodeMirror edit and diff dispatch paths now refresh the file-editor view-state cache immediately after document or selection transactions, and normal edit mode publishes selection-only share scroll frames too.
- Reproduced with `tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_share_host_editor_snapshot_tracks_codemirror_cursor_after_typing`, which failed with `cachedAnchor: 0` after a CodeMirror edit in an active share and now asserts the outgoing share snapshot carries the live cursor. Host-authored `finder` UI-state frames still move the client to the new session.
