## 2026-06-12

### Tmux, Terminal, YO!share, and Tabber

#### DOIT.69 YO!share host-authoritative terminal grid
- Completed and removed `DOIT.69.md`. Share-view terminals now size only from the host PTY rows/cols; if host dimensions are unavailable, the viewer skips local resizing instead of estimating from its own pane box or viewport. Host dimension changes resize the viewer xterm, call `reset()` on actual row/col changes, and repaint from the host-sized grid instead of preserving smeared rows.
- The share upstream resize path now requests `tmux refresh-client` after `set_pty_size`/SIGWINCH so host resize events produce a clean tmux repaint for viewers. Geometry-drift resync also reapplies terminal dimensions, so a drift repair can re-pin the terminal grid rather than only relaying layout/chrome.
- Read-only share viewers now have a stronger host-owned scroll contract: scroll publishing is impossible from read-only viewers, local scroll events restore directly to the last host-authored value, pending Finder/Differ/Preferences/editor scroll frames replay after pane rebuilds, and read-only mirrored scrollbars/client-only Preferences chrome stay hidden so the client remains visually host-identical.
- Topbar menu restoration republishes the popup layer after rerenders, keeping File/tmux/Tabs/language hover-open menus and option highlights on the same host-owned popup path. The localization sidecar moved additional visible frontend strings, including share mirror status, disabled/admin labels, tmux-window labels, file-drop insertion statuses, editor fallback/error text, Markdown task checkbox labels, and HTML preview title, into locale keys.
- Verification for this archive entry: `python3 tools/static_build.py`, `python3 tools/static_build.py --check`, `node tests/layout_url.test.js`, `python3 -m pytest tests/test_server_query.py::test_share_viewers_receive_host_terminal_dimensions -q`, `python3 -m pytest tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_share_readonly_diff_scroll_and_popup_mirror_are_host_owned -q`, full `python3 tools/check.py` outside the sandbox (`CHECK PASSED in 14.77s`), and dev1 restart/smoke on port 8001 (`ping: 401 0.042744s`).

#### DOIT.68 YO!share mirror state and popup parity regressions
- Completed and removed `DOIT.68.md`. Read-only YO!share clients now mirror host-owned editor diff state instead of falling back to plain editor content: diff mode, FROM/TO refs, per-editor unchanged expansion, vertical/horizontal scroll, and selection are carried in share UI/scroll frames and restored before or after the CodeMirror scroller exists.
- Client input over mirrored editors, Finder, and Differ stays passive. Host-authored scroll frames are the only authority for read-only restoration, while client hover, focus, wheel, scroll, keyboard, and pointer events are blocked before local pane/Dockview/Finder/editor handlers can publish or snap back to top.
- Tabs dropdowns, menu option hover/highlight, tab hover popovers, diff-ref dropdowns, and other host popups now mirror through the popup-layer channel as sanitized inert HTML. Popup selectors cover detached and inline tab popovers, app menu commands carry a real `share-mirror-active` class, and owner/sequence handling keeps stale frames from resurrecting closed host UI.

#### DOIT.67 YO!share mirror completeness follow-ups

- Mirrored popups now mount under the scaled app root, use host app-space rectangles, inherit the app font, and reset direct-child positioning/visibility/transform so app menus, tab hover popovers, context menus, and the YO!share modal render once through the root mirror transform. The 024/025 popup drift was the direct-child popup CSS re-anchoring itself from the host rect; the shared mirror-shell reset fixes that instead of patching YO!share only.
- Read-only share viewers now treat host scroll as authoritative for editors, Finder, and Differ: wheel/touch/keyboard/scroll input over mirrored app surfaces is blocked or restored to the last host-authored scroll frame while selection, browser copy, and context-copy stay available.
- Host language changes are carried in share appearance snapshots and live appearance frames, and applying a mirrored language frame re-renders chrome, menus, popovers, Finder/Differ labels, and open pane UI without blanking Differ rows. User-facing language choices show names/endonyms only; raw locale codes stay in data/payload/debug surfaces.
- The 022/023 pane screenshots showed viewer-only/read-only chrome and stale local state as the first visible mismatch, not a pane split-ratio defect. Geometry coverage remains on the shared digest (`viewport`, slots, tab strips, terminal cells, editors, fonts) plus the browser popup geometry check.

Viewer resize changes only the mirror transform, not host tmux dimensions.

Share records now carry every tmux session from the pane/tab layout, `/share/<id>` bootstraps all of them, share websockets allow exactly that session set, and viewer caps count distinct viewer browsers rather than the number of terminal sockets opened for that layout. #### DOIT.65 Differ tab home and physical-file editor identity
- Completed and removed `DOIT.65.md`. Re-opening an existing file/diff editor now activates the tab in the pane where the user last put it; normal Finder, Differ, Quick Search, and context-menu opens do not silently rehome an existing editor to the active/first/leftmost pane. Explicit file drag/drop still opts into rehoming with `rehomeExisting: true`.
- Editable text editors are now unique by backend physical-file identity, not path string. The backend emits safe `realpath`, `file_id`, and `file_identity` fields from `stat()` through list/read/write/search/path-info payloads; blocked symlink escapes and broken symlinks expose no editable identity. The frontend records display-path-to-identity and identity-to-primary-open-path mappings, folds real-path/symlink/hard-link aliases into the existing editor, preserves dirty buffers, switches to the requested edit/diff mode, and dedupes rapid same-path open races through an in-flight open promise.
- Differ context-menu Open actions are listed first in the requested fixed order: `Open in a Differ`, `Open in a new Differ`, and `Open in a new Editor`. Repeat Differ row clicks now apply the final Diff/Edit decision to the actual opened editor item, so a tab that was briefly or manually in Edit mode returns to Differ view. README and `docs/specs/GUI.md` document the pane-home and physical-identity contracts.
- Verification: `python3 tools/static_build.py`, `python3 tools/static_build.py --check`, `node --check static/yolomux.js`, `node tests/layout_url.test.js`, `python3 -m pytest tests/test_filesystem.py -q` (60 passed), `python3 -m pytest tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_differ_reopen_keeps_dragged_file_tab_home tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_dockview_symlink_alias_focuses_existing_file_editor -q` (2 passed), and unsandboxed `python3 tools/check.py` (`CHECK PASSED in 15.73s`; an earlier full run had one browser xdist timing failure that passed focused and on rerun). Restarted `yolomux-dev2-8002.service`; live 8002 verification confirmed the served bundle/locale changes, a moved `filediff:/repo/app/src/live-main.py` stayed in `slot2` after reopen, and a real path plus symlink alias focused one dirty editor.

#### DOIT.63 terminal hard-wrapped URL links
- Completed `DOIT.63.md`. Terminal URL link stitching now handles ink/TUI-style hard wraps where each visual URL row is emitted as a separate non-`isWrapped` line, including zero-indent continuations at terminal width or width-1. The continuation guard still rejects a following fresh `https://`, `file://`, or `www.` row and still refuses to merge when the previous row did not reach the terminal edge.

#### DOIT.64 Differ click and duplicate-editor follow-up
- Differ row clicks now request the Diff editor even for transcript-touched `T` rows when the file can render a real repo diff. If the diff fetch or renderability check fails, the editor falls back to Edit with a visible `diff unavailable: ...` status instead of silently looking like a normal editor open. Differ row opens start with collapsed unchanged context through a per-editor override, so clicking a Differ row no longer changes the global persisted diff expansion setting.
- The Differ row context menu now exposes `Open in a new Diff Editor` first and `Open in a new Editor` second, through locale keys in every shipped catalog. Background file reloads now capture/restore each same-file editor tab's CodeMirror selection and scroll, and push/watch reloads defer replacement while any editor for that path has focus or the file was just saved/returned to clean.

#### DOIT.57 terminal file-action menu completed
- Completed and removed `DOIT.57.md`. Terminal file drops now route through one shared `DROP_ACTIONS` registry across drag/drop, uploads, paste, and command-palette actions. The P2/P3/P4 work added read-only shell actions (`file`, `wc`, `tail -F`, `jq`, `column -t`, directory size scans), multi-file prompt actions, per-category last-action memory, Upload Preferences for read-only shell autorun and custom action lines, command-palette file actions for the active file/selection, and shared Finder/Explorer/Differ/Tabber image-row `Copy image` context-menu behavior.
- Image paste/drop option order is now exposed in Upload Preferences through `uploads.image_action_order`. The default puts agent OCR, screenshot diagnosis, image description, and `info` first so the `1..9` popup starts with the common operations; the Preference stores prompt actions as `Popup label: ; prompt text`, supports non-AI rows such as `info`, caps the list at 9, and is authoritative for image menus so undeclared fallback actions are not appended. The pasted image path/reference is inserted before the menu, so `Insert path` is not included in the image action order; stale `Server: OCR image` and `Show file type` rows are dropped.
- Server-side read-only runners now live behind `POST /api/drop-action/run`: bounded file info, text preview, log error/warning scans, CSV/TSV/JSON/NDJSON data stats with a small text chart, and OCR via `tesseract` when available. The route delegates through the app layer and the runners use the existing filesystem validation/credential guards.

#### Editor scroll preserved across tab switches
- Completed and removed the unnumbered `DOIT.md` (markdown editor scroll snap). Editor scroll/selection now survives a Dockview tab switch away and back (`2026.md` -> Preferences -> `2026.md`); the prior behavior snapped the editor to the top of file. `captureFileEditorPanelViewState()` stores a CodeMirror `scrollSnapshot` plus `scrollTop`/`scrollLeft`/selection; CodeMirror scroll events schedule a shared `scheduleFileEditorPanelViewStateCapture(item, panel)` so "scroll, then switch away" persists state regardless of tab-event order; Dockview tab `pointerdown`/`mousedown` runs `captureDockviewPreviousPaneBeforeTabActivation(...)` before Dockview switches panels (manual Dockview tab clicks bypass `activatePaneTab()`); and `fileEditorPanelViewStateCaptureHasLayout()` blocks a pooled/disconnected/zero-height pane from overwriting a good saved scroll with `scrollTop: 0`. Restore reapplies after CodeMirror focus and across animation frames. `docs/specs/GUI.md` records the tab-switch scroll contract, distinct from the existing background-reload contract.
- Shipped on `main` as `a352c3b fix: preserve editor scroll across tab switches`. Real-click regressions in `tests/test_browser_layout.py` use real DOM tab clicks rather than `activatePaneTab()`: `test_long_markdown_editor_scroll_survives_dockview_tab_click_roundtrip`, `test_preferences_scroll_survives_dockview_tab_click_roundtrip`, `test_info_scroll_survives_dockview_tab_click_roundtrip` (`3 passed`). Also `node tests/layout_url.test.js`, `python3 tools/static_build.py --check`, `node --check static/yolomux.js`.

### Editor, Finder, Differ, and Files

#### DOIT.63 hover focus no longer retargets Finder/Differ context

Dockview tab click and Enter/Space activation now commit explicit tmux interaction at the gesture site, preserving click/type behavior while preventing auto-focus hover from changing Finder/Differ session context.

Fresh/default and `sessions=`-only layouts now dock Finder/File Explorer by default; explicit Finder hide actions share a localized status message showing the restore shortcut; Dockview adoption re-docks Finder when a non-user layout commit drops it while preserving the previous Finder slot when possible; and the legacy small-slot prune protects any slot containing Finder, even as a background tab.

#### DOIT.58 D1-D3 Differ target must not follow hover auto-focus
- Audit + guard: the Differ's committed target session (`fileExplorerChangesSelectedSession` / `fileExplorerExplicitSyncSession`, read by `fileExplorerSessionFilesTargetSession()`) is moved only by explicit user intent. Verified the explicit/passive split is already correct in the code: `setFocusedTerminal` commits (`rememberFileExplorerExplicitSyncSession` + `scheduleFileExplorerActiveTabSync`) only when `options.userInitiated === true`; the hover chain (`selectPanelOnHover` -> passive `setFocusedTerminal` + `focusTerminalWhenAutoFocus` -> `term.focus()` -> the `onFocus`/`focusin` passive `setFocusedTerminal`) never passes that flag, and no `fetchSessionFiles({destination:'finder'})` call uses raw `focusedTerminal`/`focusedPanelItem`. So D1 needed no code change — the regression is already absent.
- D2 tests: extended the existing hover guard in `tests/layout_url.test.js` to cover full Differ mode (`fileExplorerMode === 'diff'`) — with session A committed, `selectPanelOnHover(B)` + passive `setFocusedTerminal(B)` + passive `selectSession(B)` all keep the Differ target on A (the source for title / session-select / cache key / fetch), while `selectSession(B, {userInitiated:true})` commits it.
- D3 docs: `docs/specs/GUI.md` Finder/Differ rules codify the explicit-intent contract. (The level-3 Tabber row pipeline already routes through the committed target, so it inherits the same guarantee.)

#### DOIT.58 Tabber — the Finder pane's third mode (B1-B6, level 3)
- New `Finder / Differ / Tabber` mode of the one shared file-pane control (`fileExplorerMode` extended to `files|diff|tabber`; `normalizeFileExplorerMode`/`readStoredFileExplorerMode` accept it; a third toggle segment; body class `file-explorer-mode-tabber` takes over the pane like Differ). The Tabber is a live tree of everything open: tmux sessions (level 0) -> their windows (`index:process`, agent-tinted, level 1) -> each window's panes (process + cwd basename, level 2) -> the touched paths grouped by repo with the git branch on the repo row (level 3, lazily fetched from `/api/session-files` and cached locally when a session is expanded, so it never disturbs the Differ target).
- Rows render through the SHARED Finder/Differ row pipeline (`renderTreeChildren` -> `updateFileTreeRow` -> `updateFileTreeRowContents`) via a `mode:'tabber'` render option whose per-row display values are precomputed as data — no forked `*RowHtml` builder. Expansion is a persisted set keyed by STABLE id-based node paths (`s_<session>/w_<index>/p_<index>/r_<n>/f_<n>`), so a session add/remove never shifts another node's expansion. `renderTreeChildren` gained a data-driven `expandedSet` option (no mode branch).
- Sort + time column come from the activity ledger (`GET /api/activity`, polled only while the Tabber is open): a session/window row's recency is `max(last_user_input_ts, last_agent_active_ts)`, set as the entry's `mtime`; the tree sorts most-recent-first (`treeSortMode:'newest'`) with the shared `None/Date/Ago` date column, re-sorting on poll without collapsing expansion. Row actions: session click focuses the session, window click switches the tmux sub-window (`tmuxWindow({windowIndex})`), context-path click opens the file (diff) in the focused pane, repo click roots Finder at the repo.
- Docs: `docs/specs/GUI.md` gained a `Tabber Pane Rules` section + Terms note; README gained a Daily-use bullet. Tests: a `t@tabber` node test renders the DOM (sessions/windows/panes, double-render reuse, recency sort, level-3 repo + openable file rows) and asserts the human labels, never the synthetic node keys; `test_browser_layout` mode list updated to the 3-way toggle. Shipped across `0.3.1`-`0.3.4`. The later D1-D3 Differ-target work is archived above.

#### DOIT.59 Uploads default into a `.uploads/` subdir
- Browser uploads (drag-drop onto a terminal, clipboard paste, the `+` button) now write into `<resolved-dir>/.uploads/` by default instead of the cwd / repo root, so pasted screenshots and dropped files stay out of source and are easy to clear. New `uploads.subdir` Preference (default `.uploads`; empty string opts back into the old cwd behavior, allowed via a `STRING_ALLOW_EMPTY` set so a blank value isn't reverted like other empty strings). One owner: `upload_target_dir` split into `_resolve_upload_base_dir` (the old resolution) + a single `_apply_upload_subdir` that reads the setting, rejects absolute / `..` escapes, `mkdir 0o700`, and falls back to the bare resolved dir on failure with the home-guard preserved; every upload caller already routes through it, so no per-call-site fork. Preferences field added in `80_panes_preferences.js` + `pref.uploads.subdir.{label,help}` across all 13 locales. Tests: 4 `_apply_upload_subdir` cases (default / empty / escape / uncreatable) in `test_app.py` + 3 sanitize cases in `test_settings.py`; 564 pytest green. Documented via the Preferences help text; README has no uploads-destination section and `docs/specs/GUI.md` had unrelated in-flight edits, so no separate persistent-doc note was added.

## 2026-06-10

### Tmux, Terminal, YO!share, and Tabber

#### Terminal copy while Claude is running (OSC 52 clipboard bridge + right-click highlight)
- Root cause of "copy does nothing while Claude runs": while a TUI owns the mouse, a drag never makes an xterm selection — the copied text leaves the app as an OSC 52 clipboard escape. tmux's default `set-clipboard external` DROPS application OSC 52, and even when forwarded, xterm.js ignores OSC 52 without a registered handler. Verified empirically on a scratch tmux 3.4 server (`external` drops, `on` forwards) and end-to-end on the live server (OSC 52 from a pane reached the attached client PTY and decoded to the exact text).
- Fix: `bridge_tmux` ensures `tmux set-option -s set-clipboard on` before each attach (idempotent, self-healing); new `installTerminalOsc52Bridge` registers an OSC 52 parser handler that decodes base64 UTF-8 and writes the browser clipboard through one shared chain (`writeTerminalTextToClipboard`: synchronous `copy` event first, then async `navigator.clipboard`). `?` read-queries are consumed unanswered (no clipboard exfiltration).
- Shortcuts: Cmd-C/Ctrl-C copies the xterm/browser selection; Cmd-C with no selection is swallowed with a how-to-select hint (Option/Shift-drag) and never reaches Claude; plain Ctrl-C with no selection still sends SIGINT; explicit tmux copy-mode copy is Cmd-Option-C (Mac) / Ctrl-Alt-C (PC) plus a right-click menu item.
- Right-click no longer clears the terminal highlight: a capture-phase right-mousedown captures the selection and stops xterm from clearing it; the context-menu Copy uses that captured text.
- Opt-in copy-path instrumentation behind storage key `yolomux.debugCopy`.
- Verification beyond the standard gate: live-confirmed by the user (copy while Claude running, Cmd-C on an Option-drag selection, SIGINT fallthrough, right-click highlight, tmux-copy shortcut/menu); node OSC 52 decode/handler/clipboard + right-click + SIGINT guards; full pytest 481 passed.

### Editor, Finder, Differ, and Files

#### DOIT.53 active-pane Quick Open, pane chrome, Finder/Differ toolbar, and working-state polish archived
- Completed and removed `DOIT.53.md`. Cmd-P normal file opens now target the pane that owns the active tab while explicit split-open keeps split behavior; the session agent badge moved from the top tab-title row to the pane Info Bar; the pane-header detail toggle now says Show/Hide details instead of YO!info and syncs title/aria/pressed state; tmux panes render a per-window button bar with duplicate-name disambiguation and numeric overflow fallback; Codex working-state detection treats bottom composer/model-status chrome as chrome so the YO marker spins while the agent is actually working.
- Finder and Differ now share `Date | Expand all | Collapse all | Reload` toolbar controls through one parent path. The Expand/Collapse buttons use skinny in/out arrow SVG icons, stay narrow in all toolbar contexts, and Sync-mode Expand is bounded to affected sync-plan paths such as `yolomux.dev2` instead of recursively crawling broad home roots. Verification beyond the standard gate: the focused Finder Sync browser regression.

### UI, Theme, Preferences, and Localization

#### Dockview drag/drop hardening and GUI behavior spec

- Restored right-root drops for stacked panes without stealing normal local pane-edge splits by using a wider cross-gutter tolerance for full-span root drops. Left and right root-edge previews now create full-height panes beside stacked content, while local pane-edge drops still split only the target pane.

### Build, Refactor, Docs, and Tests

#### Refactor audit: one-source dedup, lint enforcement, god-file split (DOIT.53 refactor batch)
- Post-Dockview-rewrite refactoring audit, 39 items. (The DOIT.53 *number* was reused after the 06-09 "Differ selection/delete" batch below — this is unrelated work.) Collapsed divergent copies into single owners: approval-prompt detection moved into `yolomux_lib/approvals.py`, which de-inverts `app.py`'s import of the root `auto_approve_tmux` CLI (one shared detector, guarded by an `is`-identity parity test); one `TtlCache` behind the metadata + transcript-lookup caches; `yolomux_lib/atomic_file.py` for the flock+atomic-write idiom (adds the fsync one of the three copies lacked); shared `cmd_error` and `git_ahead_behind_counts`.
- Backend boilerplate folded into helpers (`write_app_result`, `write_validated_int_result`, `require_known_session`). Frontend shared parents: `dedupeInflight` (one cache+inflight fetcher), `paneTabInnerHtml` (Dockview + DOM tab builders), `panelDomId`/`terminalDomId`/`transcriptDomId` id helpers, `delegate()` for per-render listener loops. Split the two ~5k-line god-files into `45_file_explorer_actions.js` and `95_codemirror_editor.js` (bundle byte-identical).
- CSS: theme-aware `--shadow-rgb` (shadows now flip in light mode), `--text-muted-strong` (was `#8b95a5` in 6 places), one grouped truncation rule; `tmux-wall.css` tokens realigned to the app's.
- Enforcement added: `tools/check.py` runs the whole CPS gate as one command; `static_build.py` gained undefined-CSS-var + duplicate-declaration lints (caught and fixed 6 live bugs); the node suite got a `test()` runner so a failing assertion no longer aborts the rest and prints a pass/fail summary; `tests/ui_pins.json` + `test_ui_pins.py` are a single source for shared color pins with a drift guard; `page_html`/`app_css` de-dup the Selenium fixtures.
- Live bugs fixed along the way: `tmux_utils` used `time.sleep` without importing `time` (crashed highlight-moving auto-approve); `tmux_wall` capture dropped `-J` (wrapped lines rendered wrong); the 6 undefined CSS vars the new lint surfaced.
- Also stripped ~470 ephemeral `DOIT.N` tags from code comments (the rationale stays; reference the persistent docs instead, since DOIT files are deleted when done). Verification beyond the standard gate: `tools/check.py` green — 534 pytest, node suite exit 0, `static_build --check`, both `node --check`, whitespace clean. Shipped at 0.2.81. The approval-engine de-inversion (B8/G2) is covered by unit + parity tests but was not validated against a live approval flow.

#### DOIT.52 push-driven filesystem and session-file refresh archived
- Completed and removed `DOIT.52.md`. The browser polling path now has Preferences-backed refresh controls, `/api/session-files` and `/api/transcripts` serve cached/stale results with background refresh, explicit user refreshes use `force=1`, and the server exposes authenticated `/api/client-events` SSE events through `ClientEventBroker`.
- Added server-side watch/poll invalidation through `/api/watch/roots`, filesystem/settings/transcript signatures, cache invalidation, and push-only-on-change behavior. Post-push live-debug churn was reduced by coalescing session-file refreshes through the cached path, avoiding `fs_changed` session-file fetches, skipping expensive connected-client polling while renewing watch roots, keeping transcript directories on transcript watching, and preserving session-files cache across filesystem changes. The final user-provided debug sample held `/api/session-files` to 6 calls averaging 347.1ms, with remaining slow endpoints tracked separately.

## 2026-06-09

### Editor, Finder, Differ, and Files

#### DOIT Search formatting and editable Markdown tasks
- Quick Search now normalizes a trailing punctuation query such as `DOIT:` to `DOIT` for file search, ranks basename matches ahead of path-only fuzzy hits, and renders image hits in Popular IDE-style form such as `[Image #1] '/home/keivenc/yolomux.dev1/20260609-001.png'`.
- Markdown Preview now wires rendered task-list checkboxes back to the open file model: clicking a `- [ ]` / `- [x]` checkbox toggles the Markdown source, refreshes linked preview panes/popouts, updates CodeMirror documents, and uses the existing dirty/autosave path.
- Verification: standard gate green.

#### DOIT.53 Differ selection/delete and non-git diff counts
- Unified Differ file-row selection and file context menus onto the Finder shared parent: single-click, shift-click, and cmd/ctrl-click now use `updateFileTreeSelectionFromClick`, right-click file rows use `showFileTreeContextMenu`, and the shared delete path refreshes session-files so deleted Differ rows disappear immediately. Removed the Differ-only single selected-path state and safe-only file context menu.
- Added `diff_tracked` to session-files payloads. Counts from real `git numstat` stay green and contribute to repo totals; raw full-file counts for untracked/no-repo files stay visible per row but render neutral and are excluded from added/removed totals. Transcript-touched files outside any git repo now appear under the `Outside repo` section instead of being silently dropped.
- Verification beyond the standard gate: `python3 -m pytest tests/test_session_files.py -q`. Full `python3 -m pytest tests -n auto -q` ran 454 passing tests with two failures: the YO!agent rolling-summary test passed when rerun serially, and the remaining browser failure is the pre-existing dirty-`TODO.md` diff-overview row-offset drift.

#### DOIT.52 tab-drag and Finder sync perf
- Fixed the slow tab-drop path by moving layout render decisions into one shared scheduler (`requestLayoutRender` / `performLayoutRender`) and replacing the old `pendingPanelsRender` boolean with a structured `pendingLayoutRender` request. Same-shape drag drops now keep the cheap `syncActivePanelsInPlace` + tab-strip path, while metadata-driven `renderPanels()` calls during drag still record an explicit forced-full render request.
- Reduced the Finder sync re-render floor by adding one sync-plan parent (`fileExplorerSyncPlanKey`, `fileExplorerSyncPlanAlreadyApplied`, `markFileExplorerSyncPlanApplied`) and skipping automatic repeated root+expand-path plans after they have already applied. Explicit Sync still forces a re-apply, and manual expand/collapse/root-mode changes reset the applied key.
- Aligned Finder refresh defaults by changing the JS fallback to `5` seconds and migrating exact stale saved poll defaults (`file_explorer.refresh_seconds: 1`, old round performance poll values) to the current defaults without changing nearby custom values. Did not add the optional B3 mtime sweep because `/api/fs/info` is not a cheap stat-only endpoint today; adding it to every watched directory poll would likely make the path worse unless a dedicated stat endpoint is introduced.
- Verification beyond the standard gate: `python3 -m pytest tests/test_settings.py -q`. Full `python3 -m pytest tests -n auto -q` ran 454 passing tests and one unrelated failure in `test_diff_overview_matches_actual_todo_codemirror_rows` because the already-dirty `TODO.md` changed the hard-coded CodeMirror row offset from `45531` to `45544`.

#### DOIT.51 blame popover, quick-open dedupe, worktree identity, risk labels, and drag timing
- Inline blame now uses a styled hover popover with author, absolute date, sha, summary, and optional commit body instead of a native tooltip; blame payloads include a deduped commit-body map and skip uncommitted/empty bodies.
- Quick Search collapses an already-open file to one Tabs row with edit/preview view chips, the editor navigation stack is capped at 50 entries, linked git worktrees are identified separately from their parent checkout in session metadata, YOLO risk labels normalize to the canonical display set, and tab-drag timing instrumentation is available behind the opt-in `yolomux.debugDragTiming` local-storage flag.
- README documents the `0.0.0.0` default host behavior, the local-only `--host 127.0.0.1` opt-in, and the canonical YOLO risk-label vocabulary; CLI help also reflects the host default.
- Verification beyond the standard gate: `python3 -m pytest tests/test_filesystem.py tests/test_metadata.py tests/test_yolo_rules.py -q`.

### UI, Theme, Preferences, and Localization

#### DOIT.54 Dockview pane polish and file-drag parity
- Dockview pane separators now use the shared skinny sash line instead of a fat group border; the line thickens only on hover/drag. Inactive Dockview tabs inherit the pane tab-strip background, and Dockview/root/tab/file drag previews use the configurable pane separator color.
- Dockview now lays out to the real host size, renders YOLOmux pane controls in the Dockview header row, shows a full-span root preview before root-edge drops, preserves the root-docked Finder width when tabs move between content panes, and restores Finder/Differ file drags into panes with the same dashed split preview/open-in-editor behavior as the legacy layout.
- Follow-up: default pane spacing is now 3px; the active Dockview tab container is slightly brighter; Dockview tab hover details are restored; root top/bottom tab-drag previews no longer span into the docked Finder/Differ column; and Dockview group padding reserves pane-spacing width so the active ring does not paint over terminal/xterm content.
- Follow-up after rebase: dragging a tab over another Dockview tab now shows a 24px dashed insertion box between tabs instead of a half-tab overlay on top of the target tab; the shared separator hover line is now 5px; pane-edge drops split only the target pane while root-edge/cross-gutter drops still create full-span panes.
- Follow-up after live resize review: Dockview pane-content edge drops now route through YOLOmux `splitSessionAtSlot`, so a second same-axis split preserves `1/2 | 1/4 | 1/4` instead of flattening into equal thirds. Dockview Finder/Differ sash adoption now accepts the new root Finder percentage while preserving nested content split percentages, so moving the Finder/Differ column resizes Pane1/Pane2 proportionally.
- Verification beyond the standard gate: `python3 -m pytest tests/test_browser_layout.py -q -k dockview`.

## 2026-06-06

### Agents and Automation

#### DOIT.44 pending-approval roster badge
- Fixed the auto-approve-off roster path so pending permission prompts are visible without focusing the session. The cheap all-session status path now captures the discovered agent pane instead of the bare tmux session, derives `approval_prompt_state()` from the already-captured visible pane text, and still avoids the expensive hybrid transcript / full-pane prompt fan-out. The session-state classifier also treats `screen.key === "approval"` as `needs-approval`, so the roster lights `EXEC?` even if a future payload misses `prompt.visible`. Added backend coverage for cheap roster prompt visibility and non-active agent-pane targeting, plus a JS classifier regression for screen-only approval state. README now documents the pending-prompt attention badge behavior.

### Editor, Finder, Differ, and Files

#### DOIT.45 editor diff + FROM/TO ref picker on clean files
- Fixed the recurring bug where pressing `Differ` on a git-tracked file with history but a clean working tree showed no FROM/TO sha picker. The clean file's default HEAD-vs-working diff is empty, so `openFileDiffAvailable()` was false and `renderFileEditorPanel` force-exited diff mode back to edit, hiding `.file-editor-diff-ref-panel`. Extracted the force-exit into `diffModeShouldFallBackToEdit(path, state, item)` and gated it on `!fileStateHasUsefulGitHistory(state)`: a file with useful history now stays in diff mode so the picker is reachable and the user can compare arbitrary refs, while untracked / creation-only / outside-repo files still fall back to the editor. Added a JS guard for clean-with-history, no-history, and real-diff states plus a source-grep guard requiring the useful-history clause.

#### Finder/Differ quick roots and summary wording
- Kept the Finder quick-root buttons `~`, `/*`, and `/tmp` present whether Sync is pressed or not, with a browser regression that checks the buttons in both Sync and fixed-root states. The Differ comparison summary now says `{repo count} repos, {file count} files changed in '{session}'` (for example `1 repo, 84 files changed in '5'`) while keeping the existing `+/-/file-count` totals on the right; locale catalogs include the new repo-count phrase.

#### DOIT.39 correction: Finder Sync and diff toolbar cleanup
- Finder Sync now treats the focused tmux session's git root as the fallback working root when changed-file payloads have not arrived yet, ignores stale same-session payloads whose repo set no longer overlaps the focused git root, then expands and highlights affected repo roots/touched dirs once the current session-files payload lands. The Finder root toggle now displays `No Sync` or `Sync`, not `Root`. Finder diff mode now has only one visible Session select, Sort select, date-mode button, and Reload button, and identical session labels no longer render as `5 5`. Long changed-file rows now force filenames to ellipsize before the agent/diff/status/date metadata clips. Verification beyond the standard gate: `python3 -m pytest tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_legacy_changes_url_opens_finder_diff_mode tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_sync_mode_opens_common_repo_parent_and_expands_affected_dirs tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_sync_mode_empty_session_opens_home_not_stale_payload tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_finder_diff_mode_toggle_fills_pane tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_differ_long_filename_ellipsizes_before_date_column -q`.

#### DOIT.39 Phase 3.3 Finder Sync empty session home fallback
- Finder Sync now treats a tmux session with no cwd as an explicit home-root case instead of leaving the previous Finder root or trusting a stale session-files payload. The Sync plan keeps session identity even when `current_path` is empty, falls back to `homePath`, and clears stale affected-repo highlights. Verification beyond the standard gate: `python3 -m pytest tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_sync_mode_opens_common_repo_parent_and_expands_affected_dirs tests/test_browser_layout.py::test_sync_mode_empty_session_opens_home_not_stale_payload -q`.

The classes clear when Sync is turned off or the payload no longer matches the active session. #### DOIT.39 Phase 3.1 Finder Sync multi-dir expand
- Finder Sync now computes affected directories from the session-files `repos[]` plus changed-file parent dirs, roots at their nearest common ancestor, expands each affected path, and falls back to the focused repo instead of `/` when a scattered set crosses above `~`. ### UI, Theme, Preferences, and Localization

The YOLO marker stays exactly green (not routed through the accent) and editor syntax greens stay out of scope. White is the one preset whose light-mode ring (`#9aa5b3`) diverges from its fill (`#dfe5ec`) so the focused pane still reads on a white panel. Shipped on `main` as `9b0f5d5 Recolor active chrome and polish preferences`. ## 2026-06-03

### Agents and Automation

#### YO ball spins on □/✓ task lists + auto-focus records nav history (DOIT.35)
- C1: a session actively working with a Ctrl-T task list showed the YO ball NOT spinning. This Claude version renders task rows with `□` (U+25A1) / `✓` (U+2713) / `✗` / `◯`, but `prompt_detector._is_prompt_trailing_ui_line` only knew the U+2610 ballot-box family — so the task rows read as new output, `visible_agent_working` flipped to False, state went `idle`, and the spin stopped. Extended the task-row glyph class + `startswith` tuple to include `□✓✔✗✘◯`. Now the task list reads as prompt-trailing chrome and the ball spins while the agent works. Regression test covers the `□`/`✓` rows + the old `☐` form.
- C2: auto-focus didn't record back/forward history (only `userInitiated` activations did), so an auto-focus jump was invisible to Back. Added a debounced `recordAutoFocusNav` in `setFocusedPanelItem` (gated on `autoFocusEnabled`): it records the focus that LANDS after a ~500ms dwell, so rapid auto-focus flapping doesn't flood the stack and a back/forward re-activation no-ops via the consecutive-dedupe. Node guard covers the wiring.

#### Auto-approve: `extract_command` read the wrong (stale) command (DOIT.17)
- A Bash permission prompt was detected as `approval`, but `extract_command` walked its backward `● Bash(…)` search past the `─────` separator and the prior `● Done.` into the PREVIOUS step, returning that step's stale (safe) `chmod` instead of the pending `cp -r src/ dist/`. The worker then classified danger on the wrong command — a real safety hole (a dangerous `cp -r` approved on the strength of an unrelated safe command) and a cause of attention not lighting under auto-approve. Fix (detector only — the mock correctly matches real Claude): bound the `● Bash(…)` search to the current prompt block (stop at the separator/box-top), stop the box-body path at the tool description instead of folding it into the command, anchor `_SKIP_LINE` as `Bash command\b` so the `(unsandboxed)` header is always skipped, and make the Codex path accept an un-prefixed command line. Regression test (`test_extract_command_does_not_cross_separator_into_prior_step`) added; detector+worker suites 60 passed. Remaining is user-gated live validation (auto-approve ON/OFF on a real agent screen), tracked in TODO.

#### Auto-approve (YOLO) reliability
- Claude `PreToolUse` permission hook shipped (DOIT.11): `yolomux_lib/claude_permission_hook.py` decides allow/deny/ask from the agent's structured request via the existing `yolo_rules` engine (no TUI scraping, no keystrokes), with 17 tests pinning the mapping + the hard-floor + fail-safe. **Remaining is user-gated / deferred and tracked in TODO Big-Bang #1**: the manual `~/.claude/settings.json` install (must not be auto-edited), live validation, the keystroke-worker stand-down (gated on the hook being live), and the Codex `app-server` re-architecture.

### Tmux, Terminal, YO!share, and Tabber

#### Session project follows the live pane cwd, not the session-number default (DOIT.32)
- `cd`-ing a tmux pane into a different repo didn't change the displayed project — `candidate_session_cwds` listed the static session-number default workdir (session "1" → `~/dynamo/dynamo1`) FIRST, so `session_git_inventory` returned it before ever reaching the pane's live `cd`'d path. Reordered so the focused pane's live cwd (then agent/other-pane cwds) wins, and `session_workdir`/`numbered_session_workdir` are FALLBACKS used only when no pane/agent sits in a repo (a fresh shell in home still shows the dynamoN convenience default). Now the project/branch/PR follow the pane within one metadata poll. pytest covers the live-cwd-wins ordering + the fallback.

#### Dark terminal: light-on-white agent composer forced readable (DOIT.30)
- The Codex composer (light text on an ANSI-white input box) was white-on-white in the DARK terminal theme because `terminalMinimumContrastRatio` returned 1 (no adjustment) for dark — so xterm left the ~1:1 cell alone. (Light already used 4.5, which is why a light terminal auto-darkened it.) Confirmed the white box is real Codex's own composer, not the local mock renderer. Fix: dark now returns a moderate 3:1 floor — enough to force the composer to a readable foreground, low enough that intentionally-dim dark-palette text (already ≥3:1) is mostly untouched; light stays at the stricter 4.5. Node guard updated (dark 1→3).

### Editor, Finder, Differ, and Files

#### Code-audit follow-ups: readonly policy, blame lifecycle, watch-list logging, TODO drift (DOIT.34)
- #1 `/api/blame` bypassed the readonly guard (only `/api/fs/*` was blocked for readonly), so a readonly identity could read repo file history. Added `/api/blame` to the admin-only GET gate; `test_login_auth` now asserts readonly gets the same FORBIDDEN as `/api/fs/list`.
- #2 The readonly file UI offered Download / open-image even though the server 403s every `/api/fs/*` read (readonly = terminal-only). Disabled `downloadDisabled`/`openInNewTabDisabled` in readonly so the UI matches the server; node guard updated (readonly download/image-open now disabled).
- #3 Inline blame didn't annotate a file opened AFTER the toggle was already on (the ViewPlugin built before any fetch populated the cache). Added `ensureEditorBlameForPath` — on a text-editor render with blame on and the path uncached, it fetches (now deduped per path via `editorBlameFetches`) then dispatches a selection-preserving transaction so the blame plugin recomputes; the annotation appears without a manual toggle.
- #4 Watched-PR truncation logged `watched_pr_truncated` on EVERY poll. Now tracked by a `(count, refs)` signature and logged only when the capped state changes (test asserts: log once on first cap, no re-log on an unchanged poll, new log on a changed count).
- #5 TODO.md still listed DOIT.29/30/31 (and the rest of DOIT.13–33) as ACTIVE BATCHES while DONE.md archived them. Rewrote the orientation: ACTIVE BATCHES is now "none — DOIT.11–33 complete/archived; only DOIT.11's hook wiring (user-gated) remains," matching the archive.

#### Finder: symlink arrow badge + target tooltip (DOIT.31)
- Symlinks rendered identically to regular files/dirs. Backend `_entry_info` already detected symlinks (`is_symlink`, target-resolved `kind`, `kind="symlink-broken"` for dangling); added `symlink_target` via `os.readlink` (best-effort). Frontend: the file-tree row now toggles `is-symlink` / `symlink-broken` and sets a native `name → target` title (broken flagged), keeping the target-type icon (a linked dir keeps the dir icon, a linked `.py` the code icon) and overlaying a small `↪` arrow badge via `.file-tree-icon::after` — `--muted` normally, `--bad` (red) + struck-through name when broken. All colors via tokens. New `finder.symlink.broken` key in 13 locales. pytest covers the backend (dir/file/broken targets + non-symlink unflagged); node guards the row toggles + title + CSS badge.

#### Terminal: an agent hard-wrapped URL links across both rows (DOIT.27)
- A long URL that Claude's TUI HARD-wraps with a hanging indent (`…/runs/26` then a separate indented `919558600/job` row) was only linked on its first row — the continuation is its OWN logical line (`isWrapped === false`), so `terminalWrappedLineGroup`'s soft-wrap sweep missed it and the regex matched only the truncated `…/runs/26`. Fix (`10_core_utils.js`): the group walk now also stitches hanging-indent URL continuations — backward sweep extends past an indented row whose previous row's tail is an unterminated url token, and the forward build, while the joined text still ends mid-URL, pulls in following indented URL-valid rows (indent stripped for matching, recorded so the underline maps to the row's REAL columns). Gated tightly (only EXTENDS a url token running off the right edge; `terminalTailIsUnterminatedUrl` + a leading-whitespace-then-URL-char shape check) so prose and adjacent independent lines are never merged. The whole URL is now ONE clickable link, underlined across both rows, active from either row. Existing true-soft-wrap behavior preserved. Node tests cover the hard-wrap stitch (both query rows + the no-merge prompt row) and the prose-not-merged / standalone-indented-URL cases.

#### Editor back/forward moved to the global topbar (DOIT.21 follow-up)
- The ← / → editor history buttons were relocated from the per-editor-pane toolbar to the GLOBAL topbar, immediately left of the universal search box (one file-history control for the whole window, like a browser's). `createTopbarNav()` builds `#topbarNavBack`/`#topbarNavForward` (wired to `editorNavBack/Forward`); `updateEditorNavButtons()` now toggles their `disabled` from the global `editorNav` stack instead of per-pane; the per-pane `.file-editor-nav-control` template, handlers, separator slot, and CSS were removed. Nav + search center as a PAIR (`margin-inline-start:auto` on the group + `margin-inline:6px auto` on the search; logical props so RTL mirrors). Node guards updated (#29 centering + the relocation/wiring assertions).

#### Modified-files "M" badge legibility (image 046)
- The Modified status badge used the theme-aware `--accent-gold`, which flips to a dark brown (`#b7791f`) in light mode — near-black "M" on dark brown read as muddy/illegible. Switched `.changes-status-m` to the fixed bright amber `#f5c542` (matching the other vibrant fixed status-badge fills), so the near-black glyph pops in both themes.

#### AI/markdown: bare URLs become links + right-click Copy URL (DOIT.15)
- Bare http(s) URLs in rendered markdown (YO!agent replies + file previews) are now real `<a>` links: `renderMarkdownPreviewInto` sanitizes into a fragment, then `linkifyBareUrls` walks text nodes and wraps URLs in safe anchors (`target=_blank rel=noreferrer noopener`), reusing `markdownPreviewUrlAllowed` so only safe schemes link. Skips text already inside `<a>/<code>/<pre>` (code samples and existing links untouched) and drops trailing sentence punctuation. Version-proof against marked's GFM autolink missing them under the per-line source anchors.
- A long URL now wraps as ONE `<a>` (`.markdown-body a { overflow-wrap:anywhere; word-break:break-word }`) instead of shattering into plain text across lines — selectable/copyable as a unit.
- Right-click menu on links: a 4th `linkContextMenu` controller + `showLinkContextMenu`/`installLinkContextMenu` (bound in `renderMarkdownPreviewInto`) offer "Copy URL" / "Open URL", localized in all 13 locales. Verified the shipped `linkifyBareUrls` against sample DOM (2 URLs linked incl. a 90-char consent URL as a single node, code-block URL skipped, trailing dot dropped, `overflow-wrap:anywhere` computed).

#### Editor inline git blame, Popular IDE-style (DOIT.26)
- A toolbar toggle (`.file-editor-blame-panel`, green when on, edit-mode-only, persisted `fileEditorBlameEnabled`) shows a dim annotation at the END of the caret's current line: "Author, <relative time> • <summary> (#PR)". Backend `/api/blame?path=&ref=` runs `git blame --line-porcelain`, parses per-line `{sha, author, time, summary, pr}` (PR from `(#N)`, all-zero sha → "You"/"Uncommitted changes"), cached per (path, HEAD, mtime, ref). Frontend: a CodeMirror ViewPlugin decorates the caret line (recompute on selectionSet/docChanged) with `data-blame` + a `title`; the annotation renders via a `.cm-line[data-blame]::after` (no WidgetType in the bundle), colored by the theme-aware `--code-comment` token (the same gray common in Popular IDEs), `user-select:none` so it's never copied as code. Blame is fetched lazily on toggle, re-rendering open text editors. Locale key in 13 locales. Backend unit-tested (parser + real-file blame); annotation/button verified via probe. Hover is the native `title` with the full commit (a styled popover is a deferred follow-up — the bundle exposes no `hoverTooltip`).

#### Modified-files panel: collapsible repo headers (DOIT.23)
- Repo group headers in the Changes panel (`~/ai-config`, `~/dynamo/frontend-crates`, …) are now collapse toggles, mirroring the uploaded-group toggle: a `<button>` with a `▸/▾` caret, per-repo collapse state persisted by path (`changesRepoCollapsed`), the file tree omitted when collapsed. Folder-level collapse still works independently. Light + dark.

#### Quick-open palette: one row per file, not duplicate editor+preview rows (DOIT.22)
- A file open as both an editor tab and a preview tab showed TWO identical palette rows (same name + path) — `commandPaletteAllTabItems` deduped by layout-item ID, and the editor item (`fileEditorItemFor`) and preview item (`filePreviewItemFor`) are distinct IDs. Now `commandPaletteCommandItems` groups file tabs by PATH and emits ONE `file:<path>` row, surfacing the open views as `edit`/`preview`/`diff` chips (via `editorViewModeFor`); selecting it focuses the editor view. Non-file tabs (sessions, Finder/Info/Prefs/Changes) stay one row each. Chips reuse the existing `editor.mode.*`/`editor.diff` labels (no new keys) and read in both themes (contrast 7.0 light / 11.9 dark). Node test guards the grouping; chips informational for now (clickable-to-jump + RECENT-row suppression are confirm-with-user follow-ups in TODO).

#### Just-updated recency pulse reuse
- Finder, Differ, and Tabber now pulse the `.file-tree-date` cell only for the new `just-updated` `<15s` recency tier in Ago and Date modes, using the shared `.attention-pulse` parent (`attention-ring-fade`, `--red-reminder-duration`, `--red-reminder-easing`, and `attentionAnimationDelay`) instead of the old standalone `file-tree-recency-pulse` one-shot. Rows settle into the existing graduated recency colors after the pulse window, and selected/current rows suppress the pulse so their colors win. Verified with `python3 tools/static_build.py`, focused Node suites for editor preview / Tabber / share theme, and `python3 tools/check.py`.

#### Editor back/forward navigation (DOIT.21)
- Popular IDE-style editor history: ← / → buttons at the far left of the editor toolbar walk back/forward through visited files. One global `editorNav` stack records every user open via `openFileInEditor` (dedupes consecutive same-file; a new open after Back drops the forward tail; recording is suppressed during a back/forward re-open). Back/forward re-open through the normal open path (reopening a since-closed file). Buttons show once there's history and disable at the ends; the nav group keeps the toolbar visible in preview mode too. Localized in 13 locales; node test covers the stack push/dedupe/truncate/navigating-suppression logic.

#### Find panel, Preferences/editor (DOIT.14, DOIT.16)
- Find-panel toggle chips robustness (DOIT.14): the overlap was already gone (the `.cm-panel` specificity override hides CM's native text), but added belt-and-suspenders — `overflow:hidden` clips any un-collapsed text, and the chip glyph is now bound to the checkbox `name` (`:has(input[name="case"/"re"/"word"])`) instead of `:nth-of-type`, so a CodeMirror control reorder can't mis-map the Aa/.*/word glyph.
- Editor Font Size no longer flips a Preview/diff pane into an editor (DOIT.16 C1): `applyEditorWrapPreference` + `setDiffExpandUnchanged` now re-render each panel with its OWN `panel.dataset.layoutItem`, not the editor item. Preview already tracks `--editor-font-size` (C2, no change needed).
- Inactive-pane dim now covers the full pane when scrolled (DOIT.16 C3): the dim is a `.panel-overlay-root::after`, but `.preferences-body`/`.changes-body` were both the overlay-root AND the scroll container, so the dim scrolled away. Decoupled — the overlay-root is now a non-scrolling flex layer (`overflow:hidden`) and scrolling moved to an inner `.preferences-scroll`/`.changes-scroll` (scroll-position preservation retargeted). Added the "overlay-root must not scroll" convention comment + node guards. Finder/Info/editor-body were already correct (overflow on inner children).
- Preferences: "Finder font size" row moved to sit right after "Editor font size" (DOIT.16 C4).

#### Diff
- Diff "expand / collapse all unchanged" toolbar toggle (DOIT.12 B4): a diff-only button (persisted `diffExpandUnchanged`, green when on) that shows full context (omits `collapseUnchanged`) or restores the collapsed runs, in both side-by-side and unified diff; the config signature includes it so toggling rebuilds. Localized in all 13 locales.
- Diff overview-ruler ticks were misaligned and went stale after expanding an "N unchanged lines" fold (DOIT.12 B3). Now positioned from the editor's rendered geometry (`lineBlockAt`/`contentHeight`, so they track folded space; line-fraction fallback before first measure), click-to-scroll jumps to the chunk's real rendered top, and a CM `updateListener` rebuilds the ticks on any geometry/height change (incl. fold expand/collapse) on both the unified and side-by-side views.

### UI, Theme, Preferences, and Localization

#### Menu dropdowns: width/wrap fix, new-session labels, Term always offered (images 055/056)
- App-menu detail lines wrapped (`white-space: normal`), making each item 3-4 lines tall AND keeping the menu narrow (a wrapping block's max-content is ~one word, so `fitAppMenuPopover` computed a tiny width). Made `.app-menu-detail` single-line + ellipsis (`max-width: 42ch`), so the fit-width grows to the longest detail → menus are wider and much shorter; full text on hover via a `title`. Shortened the verbose "Needs me first" sort detail. Fixes both the View ▾ and tmux ▾ menus.
- New-session items dropped the useless "+" prefix (label is just "Claude" / "Codex" / "Term"); when launchable, the detail now shows the params actually passed (e.g. `--dangerously-skip-permissions`, `--dangerously-bypass-approvals-and-sandbox`) via a new `agentLaunchCommands` bootstrap map (`agent_command(agent, dangerously_yolo)` from the server) + `agentLaunchParams`.
- Term is now always offered (a plain shell is always launchable) instead of greyed "unavailable" — `available_agent_commands()` always includes `term`, so both the menu and the launch validation accept it.
- pytest covers the launch-command bootstrap + Term-always-available; node guards the no-"+" label + params detail.

#### Menu-bar: View → Sort + [S]-item reconciliation (P0)
- View → Sort tab list: Default / Needs me first / By name ordering for the Tabs ▾ navigator.
- Reconciled the P0 menu-bar [S] items: File ▾ / Tmux ▾ / Help ▾ already satisfy the design tree (ticked); the proposed Settings ▾ was decided against (folded into View ▾). View ▾ remains partial (a Panel-tabs visibility toggle + an Inactive-tabs control are the last gaps).
- NOTE: a per-pane left dropdown (a `▾` caret before each pane's tab strip) was built the same day then REVERTED at the user's request — the caret took its own line above the tab strip (wasted vertical space) and wasn't wanted; a node guard keeps `.pane-tabs-menu-caret` absent.

#### Pane/Tab search finds a session by an other-branch PR (DOIT.33)
- Pane/Tabs search couldn't find a session by a PR (e.g. `#10289`) that lives on one of the repo's OTHER branches — `tabSearchFields` only indexed `displayPullRequest(info)` (the current/default-branch PR). Extended it to also fold in `info.project.git.other_branches.branches[]` (the same data YO!info renders, already in the metadata payload — no extra fetch): each branch's name, PR title, PR number in every typed form (`#N`/`PR#N`/`PR N`/`N`, via a shared `prNumberSearchForms` helper), and Linear IDs. Searching `#10289`, `10289`, the branch name, or `DIS-2193` now surfaces the session. Node test covers the other-branch PR/branch/Linear indexing + fuzzy match.

#### YO!info color audit: sub-tab band + current-branch row (DOIT.28)
- C1: the `YO!info | YO!agent` segmented toggle band hardcoded a near-black `#11151d`, so it was a black slab on the light pane. Routed `.info-subtabs` background through `var(--panel2)` (flips light/dark); the inactive-hover white tint (invisible on light) became a token tint `color-mix(in srgb, var(--text) 8%, transparent)`; the active pill text uses `var(--pane-tab-active-text)` for consistency. C2: the current-branch row used a dim navy `#161f2c` that barely stood out on the dark table, while light mode already overrode it to the selection token. Made the base `.info-row.current` rule reuse the shared selection tokens for BOTH themes (`--file-selection-bg`/`--file-selection-text`) + an `inset 3px 0 0 var(--file-selection-border)` left accent bar (mirroring the Finder's selected-file), and deleted the now-redundant `body.theme-light .info-row.current` override. Current branch is a prominent green selection in both themes; no per-theme hardcoded overrides remain. Light-mode browser contrast guard (`info-cur`) still green.

#### YO!info table light mode (DOIT.18 C1)
- The YO!info table hardcoded dark-mode colors with NO `body.theme-light` override (missed in the AUDIT-LIGHTMODE sweep), so on the white pane the non-current rows were near-white-on-white (invisible), the header/current rows were dark bars, and the PR/branch links were low-contrast pastels. Added light overrides: rows use `--text` on the white surface, the header uses `--muted` on `--panel2`, the current row uses the pale `--file-selection-bg` tint (not a dark navy bar), and the links/`pr-status-*` get darker light-tuned variants (link #1d4ed8, passing #1a7f37, failing #c0143c, merged #8250df, closed #57606a). Verified contrast 4.8–15.4 on the light pane; added the info table to the `test_browser_layout.py` light-mode guard fixture. (C2 — a "black line below the tab bar" — was investigated and is terminal CONTENT, an agent/mock `─` rule rendered dark-on-light, not a chrome bug; a live confirm is tracked in TODO.)

#### Transcript / AI-Transcript / event-log → shared theme tokens, not hardcoded hex (DOIT.25)
- These three views were dark in light mode because they hardcoded hex instead of consuming the shared theme tokens that flip via `body.theme-light`. Routed `.transcript*`, `.summary*`, and `.event-*` through `--bg`/`--panel`/`--panel2`/`--text`/`--muted`/`--line` — so they now flip light/dark automatically with ZERO per-view overrides (the AUDIT "Durable Fix A" applied; supersedes the per-component-override style). The 6 per-type transcript tints keep their accent border but derive the bg via `color-mix(in srgb, <accent> 12%, var(--panel))`, so the tint is pale on light / deep on dark with no theme rule. The event-log command now wraps across lines (`white-space:normal; overflow-wrap:anywhere`) instead of one-line ellipsis, with the time/type columns top-aligned. Verified light: bg lum 248, dark text lum 31, pale tint, command wraps to 5 lines.

#### Adjacent pane rings touch at the seam + ring opacity default 50 (DOIT.24)
- DOIT.20 had moved the pane ring to a content-edge `.panel::after` overlay, which put an active (green) pane's ring a full gutter away from a neighboring needs (red) pane's ring (~6px white gap, image 038). Reverted the ring to the `--pane-split-gap` GUTTER BORDER, colored per state by the unified `--panel-ring-color` and faded by `--pane-ring-opacity` (kept from DOIT.20). Because it fills the pane's outer edge, an active pane and a needs pane now meet across the 1px resizer — they touch. Still one marker (no "red inside green"); the needs pulse animates the border-color. Verified: active green @0.5, needs red pulsing, active+needs red, inactive transparent, all 4px. C2: ring opacity default 70→50 (settings + JS fallback + pins). The DOIT.20 TODO eyeball note anticipated this exact "revert to the gutter border" call.

#### Pane rings → one translucent overlay + opacity setting (DOIT.20)
- The green/red/white pane rings are now ONE translucent overlay drawn over the content edge (`.panel::after`), colored by the per-state `--panel-ring-color` and faded by a new `--pane-ring-opacity` (Preferences "Pane ring opacity", 20–100%, default 70). The focus ring is no longer the real border (the transparent `--pane-split-gap` border is kept purely for inter-pane spacing). One ring permanently removes the "red inside green" nesting — a focused needs-attention pane just resolves `--panel-ring-color` to red. Default ring width 4px (`--pane-tab-panel-ring-width`) and pane spacing reverted to 4px. Verified per-state via probe: transparent (inactive), green @70% (active/typing-ready/preview), red pulsing (needs), red for active+needs and typing+yolo+needs (attention beats the yolo-ready green). Node guards updated for the overlay model; test pins moved 2→4.

#### YO!info merged-PR link purple in light mode (DOIT.19)
- A MERGED PR link in the pane detail bar / popover / summary / branch-meta rendered the generic light-mode blue (`body.theme-light .meta a` out-won the dark `.meta a.pr-status-merged{#c084fc}` on a same-specificity tie). Added `body.theme-light …a.pr-status-merged { color: #8250df }` (0,3,1) so it reads GitHub-merged purple, matching the purple MERGED tab badge; OPEN/passing/failing keep their colors. Verified: merged `rgb(130,80,223)`, passing stays blue.

#### Setup screen language picker (DOIT.13)
- The first-run setup ("Set up YOLOmux … Waiting for auth.yaml changes") screen now has the same endonym-labeled language picker as the login screen / topbar. Factored a shared `locale_field_html(current, css_class)` (login + setup), positioned `.setup-locale` top-right (RTL-aware via `inset-inline-end`). The screen was already localized server-side (Steps 1/5/6, prior commit); this adds Steps 2–4: the picker carries the choice in a short-lived `yolomux_locale` cookie (NOT a settings write — the screen is pre-auth/pre-users), `request_locale_pref()` resolves cookie → saved `general.language` and feeds both setup and login serve sites, and the existing post-sign-in `save_login_locale` makes it permanent (Max-Age=600 backstop caps a stale cookie). Verified: picker reflects the locale (ja/ar selected, ar RTL), cookie carrier resolves correctly, invalid cookie falls back to the saved pref.

#### Pane chrome — one shared, state-driven theming system (no per-button/per-bar one-offs)
- All pane-head BARS (tab strip, Info Bar, editor toolbar, CodeMirror find panel) read one `--pane-bar-bg`: the bright tab-strip green when the pane is focused, neutral gray when not — so the Info Bar/find no longer stay green when unfocused (DOIT.12 B5 / images 010/011).
- All control BUTTONS (terminal/agent pill, window-step, actions, info toggle, minimize, expand `+`, close) read `--pane-ctl-*`: rest = white (light) / near-black (dark), pressed/active = green. Killed the navy active-tab and always-green `+` one-offs (DOIT.12 B5 toolbar `.tab.active`; image 009). The agent pill is green when active, `+` is white/black.
- Light-mode tab text fixed (was white-on-white): `--pane-tab-text` dark in light, plus a dark override for the `.session-button-name/dir/detail` spans that hardcoded near-white. Added a headless contrast guard (computed text color vs tab bg) — the gap that let it ship was a browser test measuring backgrounds but never nested text colors.
- Inactive-pane dimming is ONE CSS rule keyed off the uniformly-toggled `.focused-pane` class; deleted the per-pane JS overlay + `isVirtualItem` special-casing (DOIT.12 B2).

#### Topbar
- The "big space" above the green tabs was the topbar's own cool-gray background showing where the shorter pills sit centered in a too-tall bar (DOIT.12 A1/A2). Painted the topbar the green tab-strip color (`--pane-tab-strip-bg`) in both themes so it's one continuous green with no band, tightened its height (`+4px`, `line-height:1` on the brand title), and completed the Notify-toggle active state. Guard in layout_url.
- Topbar light-mode coloring sweep (DOIT.12 A4): defined `--accent` per theme (was undefined → literal light-blue hover hairline in both themes); and light overrides for the menu-count badge halo, the near-black `.transport-warning` tooltip, the garish `#tabMetaToggle.active` green (→ `#5f9800`), and the invisible menu row separator.

#### Light mode — full surface sweep (DOIT.12 B5, all HIGH items in AUDIT-LIGHTMODE.md)
- Cleared every HIGH "dark box / invisible text on white" bug. The root cause was component rules hardcoding a dark color literal with no `body.theme-light` / `body.editor-theme-light` counterpart, so the dark value rendered on the white surface. Fixed surfaces: the whole session/tab/file hover popover (near-black-green box + pale-green text → light card, dark text, re-tinted the label/value/desc/legend cluster — the audit's "highest single fix"); the neutral session-state badges + inactive YO marker (dark-slate chips → light gray); the command palette + keyboard-shortcuts dialog (were dark-on-dark: dark fill with theme-aware `--text` → light cards, dark rows/kbd); the global-reset warning bar (cream-on-brown wash → light amber tint, dark amber text); the `.agent-icon` glyphs (white → dark); the drop-target fill, the file-missing tab (dark maroon → light error tint), the server-update banner (dark navy slab → white), the file-tree current/repo-non-main/indexed rows (near-white-green / washed-amber text → darkened) + a visible selection ring; the rename input (near-black fill with `--text` → white); YO!agent markdown code blocks (`#0b0e14` → light); and in the light editor: the image backdrop + transparency checkerboard (dark/inverted → light), the diff overview-ruler ticks + inline diff decorations (saturated/dark → matched to the light `--code-diff-*` fills).
- Made it durable: two headless `test_browser_layout.py` guards (`test_light_mode_surfaces_are_readable_not_dark_boxes`, `test_light_editor_image_backdrop_is_light`) build each surface in light mode and assert backgrounds are light AND nested text meets a real contrast ratio (≥3.0). This closes the exact gap that let the white-on-white tab text ship — the prior tests measured backgrounds but never nested text colors. Verified live with a headless computed-color probe across all surfaces (every fixed text 5–15:1 on its surface). The pane-head `.tab.active` and white-on-white tab text were already cleared via the pane-chrome refactor (above); CSS brace/parse enforcement (audit Durable Fix C) shipped as `check_css_braces()`.

### Build, Refactor, Docs, and Tests

#### Build / structural
- `10_topbar_menus.css` had a TRUNCATED `.notify-toggle.active {` rule whose body was split into the next partial — it only rebalanced by accident in the bundle (DOIT.12 B1). Completed the rule, removed the orphaned body, and added a `check_css_braces()` build step that fails on any brace-unbalanced CSS partial (with a regression test). The check immediately caught the latent split.

### Mixed and Cross-Cutting

#### Watch explicit PRs independent of sessions + notify on merge/CI/review (DOIT.29)
- YOLOmux only tracked PRs tied to an open session's branch and only displayed status. Added a PR watchlist that polls arbitrary PRs and notifies on transitions. Backend: a `github.watched_prs` list setting (`owner/repo#N` or a full PR URL) + a separate, longer `performance.watched_pr_refresh_ms` (default 60s, 15s–600s) so a big watchlist doesn't burn the GitHub rate limit; `notifications.notify_transitions` now also accepts `pr-merged`/`pr-ci-failing`/`pr-review` (new `PR_TRANSITION_KEYS`/`NOTIFY_TRANSITION_KEYS` allowlist). `metadata.parse_pull_request_ref` normalizes refs/URLs → canonical `owner/repo#N` (rejects non-github hosts, issue URLs, PR #0); `metadata.watched_pr_metadata` dedupes, caps at `WATCHED_PR_LIMIT=20`, fetches each via the existing `github_pull_request_by_number` (shared metadata cache), and reports `truncated`/`invalid`. `app.watched_prs_payload` (logs once when capped) is served at `GET /api/watched-prs`.
- Frontend: polls `/api/watched-prs` on its own runtime interval; a "Watched PRs" section in YO!info (own `#info-watched` container, reuses the `pr-status-*` badges) with a remove (×) button and an empty/truncated state; right-clicking a PR in the branch table offers "Watch this PR"; Preferences gets a GitHub section (`github.watched_prs` list field) + the `watched_pr_refresh_ms` number field. Notifications: each poll diffs the per-ref last-seen status (`watchedPrLastStatus`) and fires `pr-merged` / `pr-ci-failing` (CI flips INTO failing) / `pr-review` (decision changed) through the shared channel — toast (click opens the PR) + browser `Notification` (also click-to-open via a new `options.url` on `sendBrowserNotification`), gated by `notify_transitions`, deduped + throttled by `notifications.throttle_seconds`. First sighting of a ref only records a baseline so a load with already-merged/failing PRs doesn't storm.
- 18 i18n keys added to all 13 locales (build parity enforced). Tests: pytest (`parse_pull_request_ref` accept/reject, `watched_pr_metadata` dedupe/cap/invalid/fallback shape, settings defaults + clamp + notify-key allowlist + round-trip, `watched_prs_payload` shape + truncation log) and node (`normalizeWatchedPrRef` mirror, `watchedPrStatusSnapshot`, pure `watchedPrTransitionKeys` detector, `shouldNotifyTransitionKey` opt-in gating, wiring grep, Preferences section order Performance→GitHub→YO!agent). 348 pytest + node gate green.

## 2026-06-02 (versions 0.1.76 – 0.1.101)

### Agents and Automation

#### Auto-approve & prompt detection
- Auto-approve fires with the Ctrl-T task overlay shown below a live approval prompt (bounded-overlay break instead of treating the overlay as newer output).
- Footer-hint matching accepts multi-key + parenthetical footers (e.g. `(ctrl+b ctrl+b (twice) to run in background)`) so a live prompt stays auto-approvable.
- `capture-pane` uses `-J` so a wrapped command is captured as one logical line (a wrap can otherwise split a token and flip a danger verdict).
- YO marker spins only while working (slow, configurable period), never when idle.
- Backend safety/correctness pass (P0/P1/P2): YOLO hard-floor always-on, takeover re-acquire, send-action re-verify, worker stop-join, WS frame cap, metadata TTL + bounded cache, settings coerced-keys reporting, transcript tail windowing, and related hardening.
- DECISION (DOIT.10, resolved/archived): keep the fail-safe TUI prompt-liveness guard as-is. Rejected the "default-to-live" rework — it flips the safety bias toward typing into a stale prompt (false-positive keystrokes), which is worse than the recurring footer whack-a-mole it would fix. The footer-hint band-aid + `-J` capture are the standing solution; the recurring breakage is the correct price of failing safe.
- Reliable-auto-approve groundwork (DOIT.11, partial): the Claude `PreToolUse` permission hook (`yolomux_lib/claude_permission_hook.py`) + 17 tests landed — reuses the existing rule engine, returns allow/deny/ask programmatically (no keystrokes, no TUI scraping), fails safe. Still OPEN and user-gated (tracked in TODO Big-Bang #1): wiring it into `~/.claude/settings.json`, live validation, standing the keystroke worker down once live; Codex (`app-server` JSON-RPC) deferred.

### Editor, Finder, Differ, and Files

#### Editor, diff & markdown
- The editor is plain by default — no auto-loaded diff and no inline diff coloring on open; changes appear only in the explicit diff view (the diff button / Modified-files menu).
- Clicking a relative link in a rendered markdown preview opens+renders the target file in the same pane (with a path normalizer; out-of-root links are rejected server-side and toast).
- Tightened YO!agent markdown spacing (loose lists render compact); block cursor fills the full character cell.
- README opens in rendered preview; View→Theme re-themes open editors and terminals in lockstep; theme is chosen via macOS-style preview cards.

### UI, Theme, Preferences, and Localization

#### Internationalization (i18n)
- Extracted every user-facing string in the app to a key-based `t()`/`tPlural()` catalog — menu bar (incl. the whole tmux menu), Modified-files panel, diff-ref, comparison, file-explorer + editor toolbars, command palette, keyboard-shortcuts overlay, pane chrome, rename dialog, branch list, version banner, PR-review chips, YO!info/YO!agent panel + chat, Preferences, file-editor dialogs, file-tab tooltips, hover-popover labels, session-state labels, toasts/status lines. The `en-XA` pseudo-locale shows zero plain English except intentional proper nouns (Codex/Claude/tmux/git/PR/README/theme names).
- Shipped 12 UI locales at full key parity (build-enforced): English, Traditional Chinese, Simplified Chinese, Spanish, Japanese, German, French, Brazilian Portuguese, Russian, Korean, Hindi, Arabic — plus the `en-XA` pseudo-locale. The five least-common were parallel-translated by subagents.
- Three language entry points, all endonym-labeled, all writing the same `general.language` setting: the login-screen picker (persists after sign-in), a top-right topbar switcher, and the Preferences picker. `system` resolves against the browser locale.
- Right-to-left support: Arabic drives `dir="rtl"` (client + server-rendered shell); converted all physical margin/padding/border-left|right and text-align to logical properties so the layout mirrors under RTL with no LTR change.
- Locale-aware formatting: relative time via `Intl.RelativeTimeFormat`, dates via `Intl.DateTimeFormat` (LA timezone), counts via `tPlural`/`Intl.PluralRules`.
- Chinese brand glyphs (優/优 marker, 優樂mux/优乐mux wordmark) render and re-render on a language switch; the login screen localizes server-side; the YO!agent LLM backend gets a "Respond in <language>" directive and the deterministic backend's fixed framing localizes.

#### Drag, layout & panes
- Fixed the real tab-drag root cause — a full panel re-render mid-drag was wiping the grid and aborting the native drag; it now defers and flushes on drop.
- Tab drag-reorder works in both directions (left→right and right→left), from any pane including Preferences.
- Every pane keeps its active tab highlighted (not just the focused pane); the focused pane keeps an extra ring.
- File-menu Finder entry toggles; File→Finder/Preferences/etc. open in place.

#### Tabs, badges, search & menus
- Light-mode tab badges are legible; removed the redundant "PR" pill; killed the duplicate native tooltip on hover; the session popover shows review status and reviewer.
- The default search bar blends matching commands/tabs/settings with file results; duplicate file-search results (mirrors/symlinks) collapse.
- "Branch Info" renamed to "YO!info"; merged YO!info + YO!agent into one pane with a sub-tab toggle; Preferences gained a max-tabs-per-pane field and the Performance section sits above YO!agent.

### Build, Refactor, Docs, and Tests

#### Performance
- Tab moves no longer take several seconds: a layout change no longer re-polls the server, and same-shape changes (reorder/activate/move) swap only the affected panes in place instead of tearing down and rebuilding the whole topbar + grid. Markdown preview renders are guarded by a path+content signature.
- Completed and removed `DOIT.exit_not_exit.md`. Exit-linger fallback polling now uses a 1.5s interactive base with existing jitter, and YO!stats/debug state records tab/window removal latency from WS close or tmux pane/window events through browser removal. Verified with `python3 tools/static_build.py --check`, `node tests/layout_restore.test.js`, `node tests/editor_preview.test.js`, `node tests/layout_async.test.js`, `python3 -m pytest tests/test_app.py::test_client_status_poll_fallbacks_are_interactive_with_jitter tests/test_app.py::test_tmux_signal_event_publishes_changed_window_patch tests/test_app.py::test_tmux_signal_event_publishes_removed_window_origin tests/test_app.py::test_tmux_signal_full_snapshot_keeps_removed_window_origin tests/test_app.py::test_tmux_signal_event_does_not_force_auto_approve_poll -q`, `python3 -m py_compile yolomux_lib/app.py`, and targeted `git diff --check`.

#### Process & learnings
- Recorded recurring-failure lessons from the batch (stale-backend pitfalls, build/restart discipline, falsely-marked-done detection) and folded them into the working notes.

### Demand-aware browser and server work

- Completed and removed `DOIT.network_demand_gating.md`. One browser demand descriptor now maps visible panes, active subtabs, document visibility, and notification delivery to the canonical `core`, `status`, `files`, `activity`, `transcripts`, `yoagent`, and `attention` channels. Hidden pages close SSE and unregister pane watches when system notifications are off; with system notifications on they retain only `attention`. Visibility restoration reconnects once, refreshes current state, resumes latency sampling, and does not replay hidden deltas.
- The backend client-event broker now filters every subscriber independently while aggregate channel demand controls filesystem/transcript/activity, auto-approve/tmux, watched-PR, and YO!agent producers. Debug runtime data includes bounded sanitized per-client channel/delivery records plus published, delivered, and filtered SSE events/bytes by type. The two-client regression delivers one files event and one status event instead of broadcasting four deliveries, while live baseline payload examples show why this matters: irrelevant auto-approve snapshots were about 259 KB and filesystem snapshots about 156 KB per subscriber.
- Recurring `/api/share` backup requests now require an active share; latency and disconnected auto-status polling stop while hidden; file-index polling requires visible Finder/files search; clean hidden editors no longer retain five-second watches, while dirty hidden editors keep conflict protection. YO!stats remains visible-Debug-only on the browser and keeps its independent persistent server history. Terminal WebSocket suspension was intentionally moved to the product backlog because closing it without current-snapshot, input, resize, scrollback, and notification proofs is riskier than the completed HTTP/SSE savings.
- Focused verification passed 174 demand/layout assertions, the share and clean/dirty watch regressions, nine backend demand/accounting tests, and the repaired Node/browser lanes; the final canonical gate and live 8001 restart verification are recorded by the publishing commit.

### YO!stats automatic resolution and axis alignment

- Completed and removed `DOIT.yostats_resolution_axis.md`. Client graphs now choose a friendly automatic resolution bounded to about 120 displayed buckets: 1m/5m/15m use 1s/5s/10s, wider ranges progressively coarsen, and retained history or chart-specific limits remain authoritative. Sparse event-driven samples aggregate into continuous lines, while the shared communication-gap threshold preserves real outages instead of painting a stripe for every empty bucket.
- All chart geometry now derives the plot height from the shared SVG height and top inset, so the zero grid line, labels, data baseline, and visible bottom/X-axis border meet at the same coordinate. Server history requests remain at the finest retained tier so pending local request totals are not double-counted or discarded.
- Verification passed 175 focused Node assertions, three focused Chrome cases, all nine Node layout shards including the 24-hour outage benchmark, and all eight canonical `python3 tools/check.py` lanes in 51.01 seconds. Port 8001 was restarted from the correct worktree and its served bundle hash matches disk; live inspection confirmed `Resolution: 5s`, a continuous sparse-client line, and zero aligned to the bottom baseline.
