### YO!agent roster calm then send

- Completed and removed `DOIT.84.md`. YO!agent now recognizes the exact roster-monitor request before any model call and persists a generic `wait_roster_then_send` job: it watches only the condition-clause roster, requires every real Claude/Codex target to remain idle or done, prompt-accepting, and draft-free for ten seconds, then sends the exact redacted command once to the separately named destination.
- The existing client-event watcher remains the sole poller. A shared state-file mutation atomically claims `firing` across servers; fire-time revalidation returns a busy destination to waiting, while an ambiguous claimed send persists as failed/unknown rather than risking a duplicate. The shared localized row reports roster, quiet window, blockers, destination, and lifecycle state without exposing protocol labels.

## 2026-07-08 Bounded Quick Open indexing

## 2026-07-12 Pinned tabs and pane-cap completion

- Completed and removed `DOIT.pinned-tab-limits.md`. Pinned tabs now stay resident in their pane: minimize refuses all-pinned and one-column pinned cases with the danger status, Generic minimize moves only unpinned tabs, Vertical Side Pane minimize refuses pinned dual-role residents, and Expand gathers only unpinned tabs while preserving panes that still hold pinned tabs.
- Minimize and Expand now use the shared per-pane capacity owner. Minimize into a capped target evicts only target-side eligible LRU tabs and keeps every just-minimized tab; if the target is all-pinned or otherwise unevictable, the whole minimize is refused with no partial layout change. LRU ties now evict deterministically in pane order, and the kept/incoming active tab is never evicted even when it has the oldest timestamp.
- Pinning a pane up to `appearance.max_tabs_per_pane` shows an advisory status; unpinning clears the advisory. Lowering the cap below existing pinned tabs faithfully preserves restored/share/URL layouts without load-time error spam, then refuses future incoming tabs unless eligible unpinned overflow can be shrunk. README and `docs/specs/GUI.md` document the behavior and test owners.

## 2026-07-13 Independent YO!stats cadences and mobile keyboard v3

- Completed and removed `DOIT.async-stats-cadence.md`. The elected app now owns one non-overlapping worker per metric family: CPU at 1 second, Agent Status and GPU at 10 seconds, system memory at 60 seconds, and tokens at 10 seconds while watched or 60 seconds while idle. Repeated token demand is clamped to the active cadence. Every family persists its own partial record before SSE and reports attempts/successes/failures/late/missed/runtime independently in System.
- `statsd` remains the sole SQLite mutator. Potentially long range aggregation and JSON encoding now run in the persistent `stats-reader` process through an independent SQLite WAL `mode=ro`/`query_only` connection, with its own socket, lifecycle, cache, failure, queue, resource, and System status. Hot writes, token maintenance, rollups, and retention advance in bounded turns rather than monopolizing the writer listener.
- Sparse memory and GPU gauges use presentation-only 60-second/10-second hold at fine display resolution. Hover retains the actual source time/count, held pixels do not inflate durable samples/totals/rates/cost, and expiry/outage stays an honest gap. CPU, Agent Status, and token series remain unprojected.
- Completed and removed `DOIT.keyboard-cc-overflow-altcmd-bottom-row.md` and `DOIT.keyboard-more-toggle-jump.md`. ### Range-scaled YO!stats delivery cadence

- Completed and removed `DOIT.stats-range-scaled-cadence.md`. One shared range/zoom predicate now controls delivery for both YO!stats and YO!cost: 5m/15m views demand the one-second `stats` SSE feed, while 30m+ and fixed historical zooms omit that channel and poll once per minute. Hidden pages retain neither path. Returning to a short live view reapplies demand and immediately backfills the SSE-less interval through the existing history merger.
- The backend keeps its existing aggregate-demand guard before `publish_client_event`; a regression proves a sole coarse subscriber produces zero stats serializations/events and that publication resumes exactly once when live stats demand exists. Freshness tests pin a rendered latest coarse cell, a ticking age label, and the 68001ms cadence-plus-timeout budget below the 70-second UI limit. Collection remains independently scheduled at CPU 1s, Agent/GPU 10s, memory 60s, and adaptive tokens; only browser delivery changed.
- Existing parents checked: `clientEventDemandDescriptor()`, `setDebugGraphRange()`/`clearDebugGraphZoom()`, `jsDebugStatsPollIntervalMs()`, and `TmuxWebtermApp.merge_stats_family_record()`. Search: `rg "channels.add\\('stats'|stats_sample|jsDebugStatsPoll|syncClientEventDemand|has_demand\\("`; negative search confirmed the retired visibility-only stats-demand expression and two-value poll expression are absent, and the new predicate/poll owner each has one definition.
- Verification: generated assets and `static_build.py --check`; Node core 76/0, tmux 76/0, settings 75/0; backend demand/publish 2/0; focused real-browser cadence 1/0. The eight-lane gate passed seven lanes; its concurrent non-browser lane had one unchanged dense-history budget outlier at 1.028s versus 1.000s, then that exact test passed three isolated repetitions and the complete non-browser lane passed on bounded rerun (2,234 passed, one skipped). Automated before/after publication counts are zero coarse events and one live event. Live 8881 restart/frame counting was intentionally deferred to the integrating parent because this queue ran in an isolated worktree with an explicit no-primary/no-restart instruction.
